game-generation · Code, Design, Games, Creative

Voxel Lane Hopper

Build a stunning endless lane-crossing arcade game with roads, rivers, railroads, coins, and procedural generation — compare visual polish and complete game systems.

Prompt v1.0.0
ID: voxel-lane-hopper SHA-256: ca766ae317abdbd5… 
Build a **complete, playable, visually stunning** endless lane-crossing arcade game called **Voxel Hop** — inspired by classic hopper games (like Crossy Road's *mechanics*, but **not** its branding, characters, or art).

## Visual direction (must feel premium)

- **2.5D isometric voxel aesthetic** — chunky blocks, soft shadows, depth via offset layering
- **Vibrant sky gradient** (dawn palette: coral → lavender → deep blue) with subtle parallax clouds
- **Juicy motion**: hop squash/stretch, screen shake on death, coin sparkle particles, smooth camera lerp
- **Polished UI**: rounded score pill, coin counter with icon, clean sans-serif type (system fonts only)
- The game should look **stunning in a screenshot** — not a wireframe prototype

## Required game systems (all must work)

1. **Title screen** — animated logo "VOXEL HOP", floating character, "Press Space or Tap to Play"
2. **Grid movement** — discrete hops on a lane grid: up/down/left/right (one tile per hop, no diagonal)
3. **Lane types** (procedurally generated ahead of the player):
   - **Grass** — safe resting lanes
   - **Road** — cars and trucks moving left/right at varied speeds; getting hit = death
   - **River** — water lane with floating logs/rafts; player must be on a raft or drowns
   - **Railroad** — periodic fast train crossing; instant death if on tracks when train passes
4. **Coins** — scattered on safe tiles; collecting adds bonus score with a brief sparkle effect
5. **Scoring** — +1 per lane advanced forward; display current score and best score (`localStorage`)
6. **Camera** — follows player upward as they progress; despawn lanes far behind
7. **Infinite generation** — spawn new lane rows ahead with weighted random lane types; difficulty ramps (faster vehicles over time)
8. **Death + restart** — collision triggers particle burst + brief freeze, then game-over overlay with score and "Play Again"
9. **Controls** — Arrow keys + WASD; touch/swipe on mobile (up/down/left/right swipe zones or tap edges)
10. **Game states** — `title` → `playing` → `gameover` with clean transitions

## Technical requirements

1. Output **only** a single fenced `html` code block containing the full page. No explanation outside the code block.
2. Self-contained: embedded CSS and JavaScript only. **No external libraries, fonts, images, or CDN links.**
3. Use **HTML5 Canvas** for rendering (recommended for performance) or DOM — must run at smooth 60fps on a laptop.
4. Draw all graphics procedurally (rectangles, paths, gradients) — no sprite sheets or external assets.
5. Semantic HTML wrapper; canvas centered and responsive (scale to fit viewport, maintain aspect).
6. Do **not** use Crossy Road, Flappy Bird, Snake, Tetris, Pac-Man, or Mario names/sprites.
7. Do **not** ship a broken stub — every system above must be implemented and playable on first load.

The result should feel like a premium mobile arcade hit — charming, colorful, and immediately fun.

```html
  /* Overlays */

    opacity:0; pointer-events:none; transition:opacity .4s ease;
  }
  .overlay.show{ opacity:1; pointer-events:auto; }
  .overlay.title{ justify-content:flex-start; }

  .logo{ margin-top:14px; filter:drop-shadow(0 10px 22px rgba(0,0,0,.4)); }
  .logo .row{ display:flex; gap:6px; justify-content:center; }
  .logo .row.two{ margin-top:6px; }
  .logo b{
    display:inline-block; font-size:52px; font-weight:900; line-height:.9;
    background:linear-gradient(180deg,#fff2d6,#ffd36b 45%,#ff8f4f);
    -webkit-background-clip:text; background-clip:text; color:transparent;
    text-shadow:0 3px 0 rgba(120,60,20,.25);
    animation:pop 2.6s ease-in-out infinite;
  }
  .logo .row.two b{ background:linear-gradient(180deg,#e9d6ff,#a98bff 45%,#6f5adf); }
  .logo b:nth-child(2){ animation-delay:.08s } .logo b:nth-child(3){ animation-delay:.16s }
  .logo b:nth-child(4){ animation-delay:.24s } .logo b:nth-child(5){ animation-delay:.32s }
  @keyframes pop{ 0%,100%{ transform:translateY(0) } 50%{ transform:translateY(-9px) } }

  .tag{
    margin-bottom:8px; font-size:17px; font-weight:700; opacity:.92;

  }

  .card{
    background:rgba(24,18,44,.62);
    backdrop-filter:blur(14px); -webkit-backdrop-filter:blur(14px);
    border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.15);
    border-radius:26px; padding:30px 30px 26px; width:100%; max-width:330px;
    box-shadow:0 24px 60px rgba(0,0,0,.5); margin:auto;
  }
  .card h2{ font-size:30px; font-weight:900; letter-spacing:.5px; }
  .card h2 span{ color:#ff8f5f; }
  .stats{ display:flex; gap:14px; margin:22px 0 6px; }

  .stat .n{ font-size:32px; font-weight:900; }
  .stat .k{ font-size:11px; font-weight:700; letter-spacing:1.5px; opacity:.6; text-transform:uppercase; margin-top:2px;}
  .newbest{ color:#ffd36b; font-weight:800; font-size:13px; letter-spacing:1px; height:16px; margin-top:4px;}

    margin-top:20px; width:100%; border:none; cursor:pointer;
    font-family:var(--font); font-size:19px; font-weight:900; letter-spacing:.5px;
    color:#3a1e0a; padding:16px; border-radius:16px;
    background:linear-gradient(180deg,#ffe08a,#ffb01f);
    box-shadow:0 8px 0 #c07d0d, 0 12px 22px rgba(0,0,0,.35);
    transition:transform .05s ease, box-shadow .05s ease;
  }
  .btn:active{ transform:translateY(4px); box-shadow:0 4px 0 #c07d0d, 0 6px 14px rgba(0,0,0,.35); }
</style>

<body>
  <main class="stage" id="stage">
    <canvas id="game"></canvas>

    <div class="hud" id="hud">
      <div class="pill"><span class="lbl">Score</span><span id="hudScore">0</span></div>
      <div class="pill"><span class="coin-ic"></span><span id="hudCoins">0</span></div>
    </div>

    <div class="overlay title show" id="titleScreen">
      <div class="logo">
        <div class="row"><b>V</b><b>O</b><b>X</b><b>E</b><b>L</b></div>
        <div class="row two"><b>H</b><b>O</b><b>P</b></div>
      </div>
      <div>
        <div class="tag">Press Space or Tap to Play</div>
        <div class="hint">Arrows / WASD to hop • Swipe on mobile</div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div class="overlay" id="overScreen">
      <div class="card">
        <h2>Game <span>Over</span></h2>
        <div class="stats">
          <div class="stat"><div class="n" id="ovScore">0</div><div class="k">Score</div></div>
          <div class="stat"><div class="n" id="ovBest">0</div><div class="k">Best</div></div>
        </div>
        <div class="newbest" id="newBest"></div>
        <button class="btn" id="againBtn">Play Again</button>
      </div>
    </div>
  </main>

<script>
(function(){
"use strict";
const cv = document.getElementById('game');
const ctx = cv.getContext('2d');
const W = 480, H = 760;
function fit(){
  const dpr = Math.min(2, window.devicePixelRatio || 1);
  cv.width = W*dpr; cv.height = H*dpr;
  ctx.setTransform(dpr,0,0,dpr,0,0);
}
fit(); window.addEventListener('resize', fit);

// ---- constants ----
const COLS = 9;
const TILE = 52;
const ROWH = 34;
const baseY = H*0.70;
const HOP_TIME = 0.14;
const HOPH = 26;
const TRAINHALF = 3, TRAINLEN = 6;
const CAR_COLORS = ['#ff5a5f','#ffb400','#4fc3f7','#9d7bff','#ff7ab8','#34d399','#f97362'];

// ---- state ----
let mode = 'title'; // title | playing | dying | gameover
let t = 0;
let rows = {}, genTo = 0;
let camRow = 0;
let player, particles = [], clouds = [];
let score = 0, coins = 0, maxRow = 0;
let best = +localStorage.getItem('voxelhop_best') || 0;
let freeze = 0, deathFlash = 0;
let shakeMag = 0, shakeX = 0, shakeY = 0;

// ---- helpers ----
const clamp = (v,a,b)=> v<a?a : v>b?b : v;
function shade(hex,f){
  const n = parseInt(hex.slice(1),16);
  let r=(n>>16)&255, g=(n>>8)&255, b=n&255;
  r=Math.min(255,r*f)|0; g=Math.min(255,g*f)|0; b=Math.min(255,b*f)|0;
  return 'rgb('+r+','+g+','+b+')';
}
function proj(col,row){
  return { x: W/2 + (col-(COLS-1)/2)*TILE, y: baseY - (row-camRow)*ROWH };
}
function weighted(list){
  let s=0; for(const x of list) s+=x[1];
  let r=Math.random()*s;
  for(const x of list){ r-=x[1]; if(r<=0) return x[0]; }
  return list[list.length-1][0];
}
function drawCube(cx, baseYY, w, h, hex, dep){
  const hw = w/2;
  // right side
  ctx.fillStyle = shade(hex,0.7);
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(cx+hw, baseYY-h);
  ctx.lineTo(cx+hw+dep, baseYY-h-dep);
  ctx.lineTo(cx+hw+dep, baseYY-dep);
  ctx.lineTo(cx+hw, baseYY);
  ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();
  // front
  ctx.fillStyle = hex;
  ctx.fillRect(cx-hw, baseYY-h, w, h);
  // top
  ctx.fillStyle = shade(hex,1.28);
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(cx-hw, baseYY-h);
  ctx.lineTo(cx-hw+dep, baseYY-h-dep);
  ctx.lineTo(cx+hw+dep, baseYY-h-dep);
  ctx.lineTo(cx+hw, baseYY-h);
  ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();
}
function drawShadow(cx, cy, w, a){
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(15,12,35,'+(a==null?0.2:a)+')';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(cx+4, cy+3, w*0.6, w*0.24, 0, 0, 7);
  ctx.fill();
}

// ---- world generation ----
function addGrass(row, idx){
  const n = idx<=6 ? 0 : Math.floor(Math.random()*3.4);
  const used = {};
  for(let i=0;i<n;i++){
    const c = Math.floor(Math.random()*COLS);
    if(!used[c]){ used[c]=1; row.trees.push(c); }
  }
  if(Math.random()<0.5){
    for(let a=0;a<6;a++){
      const c = Math.floor(Math.random()*COLS);
      if(!used[c]){ row.coins.push({col:c, taken:false, ph:Math.random()*6}); break; }
    }
  }
}
function addRoad(row, idx){
  const truck = Math.random()<0.35;
  const len = truck?2:1;
  const gap = (truck?2.6:2.2) + Math.random()*1.6;
  const dir = Math.random()<0.5?1:-1;
  let speed = ( (truck?1.4:1.8) + Math.random()*0.9 ) * (1 + idx*0.02);
  speed = Math.min(speed, 6);
  const total = COLS + 4;
  const count = Math.max(1, Math.round(total/(len+gap)));
  const spacing = total/count;
  const color = CAR_COLORS[(Math.random()*CAR_COLORS.length)|0];
  row.dir = dir; row.speed = speed; row.period = total;
  row.vehicles = [];
  for(let i=0;i<count;i++){
    row.vehicles.push({ x: -2 + i*spacing, wCols: len*0.92+0.5, type: truck?'truck':'car',
                        color: truck?CAR_COLORS[(Math.random()*CAR_COLORS.length)|0]:color });
  }
}
function addRiver(row, idx){
  const dir = Math.random()<0.5?1:-1;
  let speed = (1.1 + Math.random()*0.9) * (1 + idx*0.012);
  speed = Math.min(speed, 4.2);
  const total = COLS + 4;
  const wCols = Math.random()<0.5?3:2;
  const gap = 1.7 + Math.random()*1.1;
  const count = Math.max(1, Math.round(total/(wCols+gap)));
  const spacing = total/count;
  row.dir = dir; row.speed = speed; row.period = total;
  row.logs = [];
  for(let i=0;i<count;i++){
    row.logs.push({ x: -2 + i*spacing, wCols: wCols });
  }
}
function addRail(row, idx){
  row.dir = Math.random()<0.5?1:-1;
  row.period = 3 + Math.random()*1.7;
  row.timer = Math.random()*row.period;
  row.trainSpeed = 15 + Math.random()*7;
  row.train = null; row.warn = false;
}
function makeRow(idx){
  const row = { idx, coins:[], trees:[] };
  if(idx<=4){ row.type='grass'; return row; }
  const prev = rows[idx-1], prev2 = rows[idx-2];
  let types;
  if(prev && (prev.type==='river' || prev.type==='railroad')){
    types = [['grass',3],['road',3]];
  } else {
    types = [['grass',3],['road',3.2],['river',2],['railroad',1.4]];
  }
  if(prev && prev2 && prev.type===prev2.type){
    types = types.filter(x=>x[0]!==prev.type);
    if(types.length===0) types = [['grass',1]];
  }
  row.type = weighted(types);
  if(row.type==='grass') addGrass(row,idx);
  else if(row.type==='road') addRoad(row,idx);
  else if(row.type==='river') addRiver(row,idx);
  else addRail(row,idx);
  return row;
}
function ensureRows(){
  while(genTo < player.row + 20){ genTo++; rows[genTo] = makeRow(genTo); }
}

// ---- init / reset ----
function initWorld(){
  rows = {}; genTo = 18;
  for(let r=-3;r<=18;r++) rows[r] = makeRow(r);
  particles = [];
  player = { col:4, row:0, hopping:false, hopT:0, fromCol:4, fromRow:0, toCol:4, toRow:0,
             z:0, landT:0, onLog:null, onLogOff:0, dead:false, hidden:false, faceX:1 };
  score = 0; coins = 0; maxRow = 0; camRow = 0;
  shakeMag = 0; shakeX = 0; shakeY = 0; freeze = 0; deathFlash = 0;
}
function initClouds(){
  clouds = [];
  for(let i=0;i<7;i++){
    clouds.push({ x:Math.random()*W, y:40+Math.random()*260, s:.5+Math.random()*1.1, spd:6+Math.random()*10, a:.12+Math.random()*.22 });
  }
}

// ---- movement ----
function renderCol(){ return player.hopping ? lerp(player.fromCol,player.toCol, ease(player.hopT)) : player.col; }
function renderRow(){ return player.hopping ? lerp(player.fromRow,player.toRow, ease(player.hopT)) : player.row; }
function lerp(a,b,f){ return a+(b-a)*f; }
function ease(x){ return x*x*(3-2*x); }

function hop(dCol, dRow){
  if(mode!=='playing' || player.hopping || player.dead) return;
  const baseCol = Math.round(player.col);
  let tCol = clamp(baseCol+dCol, 0, COLS-1);
  let tRow = player.row + dRow;
  if(!rows[tRow]) return;                 // stay on generated ground
  if(tCol===baseCol && tRow===player.row) return;
  const lane = rows[tRow];
  if(lane.type==='grass' && lane.trees.indexOf(tCol)>=0) return; // blocked by tree
  if(dCol>0) player.faceX = 1; else if(dCol<0) player.faceX = -1;
  player.fromCol = player.col; player.fromRow = player.row;
  player.toCol = tCol; player.toRow = tRow;
  player.hopT = 0; player.hopping = true; player.onLog = null;
  if(dRow>0 && tRow>maxRow){ maxRow = tRow; score++; }
  ensureRows();
}
function settle(){
  player.hopping = false;
  player.col = player.toCol; player.row = player.toRow;
  player.landT = 0.1;
  const lane = rows[player.row];
  if(!lane) return;
  if(lane.type==='river'){
    let found=null;
    for(const lg of lane.logs){ if(Math.abs(lg.x-player.col) <= lg.wCols/2){ found=lg; break; } }
    if(found){ player.onLog=found; player.onLogOff = clamp(player.col-found.x, -found.wCols/2+0.4, found.wCols/2-0.4); }
    else { die(); return; }
  }
  for(const cn of lane.coins){
    if(!cn.taken && cn.col===player.col){ cn.taken=true; coins++; score+=2; sparkle(player.col,player.row); }
  }
}

// ---- particles ----
function sparkle(col,row){
  const p = proj(col,row);
  for(let i=0;i<12;i++){
    const a = Math.random()*Math.PI*2, sp=40+Math.random()*90;
    particles.push({ x:p.x, y:p.y-10, vx:Math.cos(a)*sp, vy:Math.sin(a)*sp-40,
      g:220, life:.6, max:.6, size:3+Math.random()*3, color:Math.random()<.5?'#ffe9a0':'#ffc123' });
  }
}
function burst(col,row){
  const p = proj(col,row);
  const cols = ['#ff7a4d','#ffe3c2','#fff','#ff5a5f','#ffc123'];
  for(let i=0;i<26;i++){
    const a = Math.random()*Math.PI*2, sp=60+Math.random()*180;
    particles.push({ x:p.x, y:p.y-14, vx:Math.cos(a)*sp, vy:Math.sin(a)*sp-120,
      g:520, life:.9, max:.9, size:4+Math.random()*5, color:cols[(Math.random()*cols.length)|0] });
  }
}

// ---- death ----
function die(){
  if(player.dead) return;
  player.dead = true; player.hidden = true;
  mode = 'dying'; freeze = 0.4; shakeMag = 15; deathFlash = 0.25;
  burst(renderCol(), renderRow());
  if(score>best){ best = score; localStorage.setItem('voxelhop_best', best); }
}

// ---- update ----
function updateWorld(dt){
  for(const k in rows){
    const L = rows[k];
    if(L.type==='road'){
      for(const v of L.vehicles){
        v.x += L.dir*L.speed*dt;
        if(L.dir>0 && v.x>COLS+2) v.x -= L.period;
        else if(L.dir<0 && v.x<-2) v.x += L.period;
      }
    } else if(L.type==='river'){
      for(const lg of L.logs){
        lg.x += L.dir*L.speed*dt;
        if(L.dir>0 && lg.x>COLS+2) lg.x -= L.period;
        else if(L.dir<0 && lg.x<-2) lg.x += L.period;
      }
    } else if(L.type==='railroad'){
      L.timer += dt;
      L.warn = (L.timer > L.period-1.1 && L.timer<=L.period);
      if(!L.train && L.timer>=L.period){ L.train = { x: L.dir>0?-4:COLS+4 }; }
      if(L.train){
        L.train.x += L.dir*L.trainSpeed*dt;
        if((L.dir>0 && L.train.x>COLS+5) || (L.dir<0 && L.train.x<-5)){ L.train=null; L.timer=0; }
      }
    }
  }
}
function hazards(){
  const lane = rows[player.row];
  if(!lane) return;
  const rc = renderCol();
  if(lane.type==='road'){
    for(const v of lane.vehicles){ if(Math.abs(v.x-rc) < v.wCols/2 + 0.4){ die(); return; } }
  } else if(lane.type==='railroad'){
    if(lane.train && Math.abs(lane.train.x-rc) < TRAINHALF + 0.4){ die(); return; }
  } else if(lane.type==='river' && !player.hopping){
    if(player.onLog){
      player.col = player.onLog.x + player.onLogOff;
      if(player.col < -0.3 || player.col > COLS-0.7){ die(); return; }
    } else { die(); return; }
  }
}
function updateParticles(dt){
  for(let i=particles.length-1;i>=0;i--){
    const p = particles[i];
    p.vy += p.g*dt; p.x += p.vx*dt; p.y += p.vy*dt; p.life -= dt;
    if(p.life<=0) particles.splice(i,1);
  }
}
function update(dt){
  t += dt;
  for(const c of clouds){ c.x += c.spd*dt; if(c.x > W+80) c.x = -80; }

  if(mode==='playing' || mode==='title') updateWorld(dt);

  if(player){
    if(player.hopping){ player.hopT += dt/HOP_TIME; if(player.hopT>=1){ player.hopT=1; settle(); } }
    player.z = player.hopping ? Math.sin(player.hopT*Math.PI)*HOPH : 0;
    if(player.landT>0) player.landT = Math.max(0, player.landT-dt);
  }

  if(mode==='playing'){
    hazards();
    const target = renderRow();
    camRow += (target - camRow) * Math.min(1, dt*5);
    ensureRows();
    for(const k in rows){ if(+k < player.row-6) delete rows[k]; }
  } else if(mode==='title'){
    camRow += (0 - camRow) * Math.min(1, dt*4);
  } else if(mode==='dying'){
    freeze -= dt;
    if(freeze<=0){ mode='gameover'; showGameOver(); }
  }

  updateParticles(dt);
  if(deathFlash>0) deathFlash -= dt;
  if(shakeMag>0){
    shakeMag = Math.max(0, shakeMag - dt*45);
    shakeX = (Math.random()*2-1)*shakeMag;
    shakeY = (Math.random()*2-1)*shakeMag;
  } else { shakeX=0; shakeY=0; }

  document.getElementById('hudScore').textContent = score;
  document.getElementById('hudCoins').textContent = coins;
}

// ---- rendering ----
function drawSky(){
  const g = ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,0,H);
  g.addColorStop(0,'#2b2350');
  g.addColorStop(0.42,'#6d5aa8');
  g.addColorStop(0.72,'#ff9e7d');
  g.addColorStop(1,'#ffd9a0');
  ctx.fillStyle = g; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
  // sun glow
  const sg = ctx.createRadialGradient(W*0.5, baseY+40, 20, W*0.5, baseY+40, 260);
  sg.addColorStop(0,'rgba(255,225,180,.5)'); sg.addColorStop(1,'rgba(255,225,180,0)');
  ctx.fillStyle = sg; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
  for(const c of clouds){
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,'+c.a+')';
    const w=60*c.s, h=20*c.s;
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.ellipse(c.x,c.y,w,h,0,0,7);
    ctx.ellipse(c.x+w*0.6,c.y+5,w*0.7,h*0.8,0,0,7);
    ctx.ellipse(c.x-w*0.6,c.y+6,w*0.6,h*0.7,0,0,7);
    ctx.fill();
  }
}
function laneY(row){ return baseY - (row-camRow)*ROWH; }

function drawLaneGround(L){
  const y = laneY(L.idx);
  const top = y - ROWH/2, h = ROWH+1;
  if(L.type==='grass'){
    for(let c=0;c<COLS;c++){
      ctx.fillStyle = (c+L.idx)%2 ? '#7ec850' : '#77c04a';
      ctx.fillRect((proj(c,L.idx).x)-TILE/2, top, TILE+1, h);
    }
    ctx.fillStyle='rgba(255,255,255,.08)'; ctx.fillRect(-40,top,W+80,3);
    ctx.fillStyle='rgba(20,60,20,.14)'; ctx.fillRect(-40,top+h-3,W+80,3);
  } else if(L.type==='road'){
    ctx.fillStyle='#474751'; ctx.fillRect(-40,top,W+80,h);
    ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,.18)'; ctx.fillRect(-40,top,W+80,3);
    ctx.fillStyle='rgba(255,255,255,.10)'; ctx.fillRect(-40,top+h-3,W+80,3);
    ctx.fillStyle='#e9d78a';
    for(let x=-20;x<W+20;x+=34){ ctx.fillRect(x, y-2, 18, 4); }
  } else if(L.type==='river'){
    const g = ctx.createLinearGradient(0,top,0,top+h);
    g.addColorStop(0,'#4bb0e2'); g.addColorStop(1,'#2f8fc6');
    ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fillRect(-40,top,W+80,h);
    ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(255,255,255,.18)'; ctx.lineWidth=2;
    for(let k=0;k<2;k++){
      ctx.beginPath();
      const yy = top + h*(0.35+k*0.35);
      for(let x=-10;x<=W+10;x+=12){
        const off = Math.sin((x*0.08)+(t*1.6)+(k*1.7)+L.idx)*2.2;
        if(x<0) ctx.moveTo(x,yy+off); else ctx.lineTo(x,yy+off);
      }
      ctx.stroke();
    }
  } else { // railroad
    ctx.fillStyle='#9a9088'; ctx.fillRect(-40,top,W+80,h);
    ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,.12)'; ctx.fillRect(-40,top,W+80,3);
    ctx.fillStyle='#5e4a34';
    for(let x=-10;x<W+10;x+=26){ ctx.fillRect(x, top+3, 12, h-6); }
    ctx.fillStyle='#c9ccd4';
    ctx.fillRect(-40,y-9,W+80,3); ctx.fillRect(-40,y+6,W+80,3);
    if(L.warn && Math.floor(t*6)%2===0){
      ctx.fillStyle='rgba(255,60,60,.9)';
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(14, y, 6, 0, 7); ctx.fill();
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(W-14, y, 6, 0, 7); ctx.fill();
    }
  }
}
function drawTree(col,row){
  const p = proj(col,row);
  drawShadow(p.x,p.y,20,.16);
  drawCube(p.x, p.y, 12, 15, '#7a4a24', 4);
  drawCube(p.x, p.y-13, 32, 30, '#3f9d4a', 9);
}
function drawCoin(cn,row){
  const p = proj(cn.col,row);
  const yy = p.y - 12 - Math.sin(t*3+cn.ph)*2;
  const w = 5 + Math.abs(Math.cos(t*3+cn.ph))*11;
  drawShadow(p.x,p.y,9,.14);
  ctx.fillStyle='#b9760a';
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(p.x, yy, w+1.5, 13, 0, 0, 7); ctx.fill();
  const g = ctx.createLinearGradient(p.x-w,0,p.x+w,0);
  g.addColorStop(0,'#e69a10'); g.addColorStop(.5,'#ffe28a'); g.addColorStop(1,'#e69a10');
  ctx.fillStyle=g;
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(p.x, yy, w, 11, 0, 0, 7); ctx.fill();
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(255,255,255,.6)';
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(p.x - w*0.3, yy-3, w*0.25, 3, 0, 0, 7); ctx.fill();
}
function drawVehicle(v,L){
  const p = proj(v.x, L.idx);
  const w = v.wCols*TILE*0.86;
  const h = v.type==='truck'?28:24;
  drawShadow(p.x,p.y,w*0.42,.22);
  if(v.type==='truck'){
    const cabW = w*0.32;
    const cx = L.dir>0 ? p.x + (w/2 - cabW/2) : p.x - (w/2 - cabW/2);
    drawCube(p.x, p.y, w, h*0.86, '#e6e9ef', w*0.12);   // box
    drawCube(cx, p.y, cabW, h, v.color, w*0.12);         // cab
    ctx.fillStyle='#2a2f45';
    ctx.fillRect(cx-cabW*0.32, p.y-h+3, cabW*0.64, h*0.4);
  } else {
    drawCube(p.x, p.y, w, h, v.color, w*0.14);
    ctx.fillStyle='#2a2f45';
    ctx.fillRect(p.x-w*0.28, p.y-h+3, w*0.56, h*0.42);
    ctx.fillStyle='rgba(255,255,255,.35)';
    ctx.fillRect(p.x-w*0.28, p.y-h+3, w*0.56, 3);
  }
  ctx.fillStyle='#20202a';
  ctx.fillRect(p.x-w*0.4, p.y-4, w*0.16, 5);
  ctx.fillRect(p.x+w*0.24, p.y-4, w*0.16, 5);
  ctx.fillStyle = L.dir>0 ? '#fff2a0' : '#ff6b6b';
  ctx.fillRect(L.dir>0?p.x+w*0.44:p.x-w*0.5, p.y-h*0.6, 4, 5);
}
function drawLog(lg,L){
  const p = proj(lg.x, L.idx);
  const w = lg.wCols*TILE*0.9, h = 16;
  drawShadow(p.x,p.y,w*0.42,.16);
  drawCube(p.x, p.y, w, h, '#8a5a2b', w*0.1);
  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(60,35,15,.5)'; ctx.lineWidth=2;
  for(let i=1;i<lg.wCols;i++){
    const lx = p.x - w/2 + (w/lg.wCols)*i;
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(lx, p.y-h); ctx.lineTo(lx, p.y); ctx.stroke();
  }
}
function drawTrain(L){
  const p = proj(L.train.x, L.idx);
  const w = TRAINLEN*TILE, h = 32;
  drawShadow(p.x,p.y,w*0.4,.28);
  drawCube(p.x, p.y, w, h, '#39405a', 10);
  ctx.fillStyle='#ffe58a';
  for(let x=p.x-w/2+16; x<p.x+w/2-14; x+=30){ ctx.fillRect(x, p.y-h+8, 16, 11); }
  ctx.fillStyle='#fff7c8';
  ctx.fillRect(L.dir>0?p.x+w/2-6:p.x-w/2+2, p.y-h*0.6, 5, 7);
}
function drawPlayer(){
  if(player.hidden) return;
  const rc = renderCol(), rr = renderRow();
  const p = proj(rc, rr);
  const idle = mode==='title' ? Math.sin(t*2.5)*3 + 3 : 0;
  const z = player.z + idle;
  drawShadow(p.x, p.y, 15*(1-Math.min(0.4, z/120)), 0.22*(1-Math.min(0.6,z/90)));
  let sx=1, sy=1;
  if(player.hopping){ const s=Math.sin(player.hopT*Math.PI); sy=1+0.25*s; sx=1-0.14*s; }
  if(player.landT>0){ const k=player.landT/0.1; sy=1-0.26*k; sx=1+0.26*k; }
  const w=30*sx, h=30*sy, bx=p.x, by=p.y-z;
  drawCube(bx, by, w, h, '#ff7a4d', w*0.3);
  ctx.fillStyle='#ffe3c2';
  ctx.fillRect(bx-w*0.26, by-h*0.5, w*0.52, h*0.4);
  // eyes
  const ex = player.faceX>=0 ? 0.02 : -0.02;
  ctx.fillStyle='#fff';
  ctx.fillRect(bx-w*0.24+ex*w, by-h*0.86, w*0.18, h*0.2);
  ctx.fillRect(bx+w*0.06+ex*w, by-h*0.86, w*0.18, h*0.2);
  ctx.fillStyle='#26120a';
  ctx.fillRect(bx-w*0.20+ex*w, by-h*0.80, w*0.09, h*0.1);
  ctx.fillRect(bx+w*0.10+ex*w, by-h*0.80, w*0.09, h*0.1);
  // beak
  ctx.fillStyle='#ff9e2c';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(bx-4, by-h*0.5); ctx.lineTo(bx+4, by-h*0.5); ctx.lineTo(bx, by-h*0.38);
  ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();
}
function drawParticles(){
  for(const p of particles){
    ctx.globalAlpha = Math.max(0, p.life/p.max);
    ctx.fillStyle = p.color;
    ctx.fillRect(p.x-p.size/2, p.y-p.size/2, p.size, p.size);
  }
  ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
}
function render(){
  drawSky();
  ctx.save();
  ctx.translate(shakeX, shakeY);

  const topR = Math.ceil(camRow + (baseY+70)/ROWH);
  const botR = Math.floor(camRow - (H-baseY+70)/ROWH);
  const pr = Math.round(renderRow());
  for(let r=topR; r>=botR; r--){
    const L = rows[r];
    if(!L) continue;
    drawLaneGround(L);
    if(L.type==='grass'){
      for(const cn of L.coins) if(!cn.taken) drawCoin(cn, r);
      for(const c of L.trees) drawTree(c, r);
    } else if(L.type==='road'){
      const list = L.dir>0 ? L.vehicles : L.vehicles.slice().reverse();
      for(const v of list) drawVehicle(v, L);
    } else if(L.type==='river'){
      for(const lg of L.logs) drawLog(lg, L);
    } else if(L.type==='railroad'){
      if(L.train) drawTrain(L);
    }
    if(r===pr) drawPlayer();
  }
  drawParticles();
  ctx.restore();

  if(deathFlash>0){
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,'+Math.max(0,deathFlash/0.25*0.5)+')';
    ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
  }
  // subtle vignette
  const vg = ctx.createRadialGradient(W/2,H/2,H*0.3, W/2,H/2,H*0.72);
  vg.addColorStop(0,'rgba(0,0,0,0)'); vg.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,.28)');
  ctx.fillStyle = vg; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
}

// ---- loop ----
let last = performance.now();
function loop(now){
  let dt = (now-last)/1000; last = now;
  if(dt>0.05) dt = 0.05;
  update(dt);
  render();
  requestAnimationFrame(loop);
}

// ---- UI / states ----
const titleScreen = document.getElementById('titleScreen');
const overScreen  = document.getElementById('overScreen');
const hud = document.getElementById('hud');
function startGame(){
  initWorld();
  mode = 'playing';
  titleScreen.classList.remove('show');
  overScreen.classList.remove('show');
  hud.classList.add('show');
}
function showGameOver(){
  hud.classList.remove('show');
  document.getElementById('ovScore').textContent = score;
  document.getElementById('ovBest').textContent = best;
  document.getElementById('newBest').textContent = (score>0 && score>=best && score===best) ? '★ NEW BEST!' : '';
  overScreen.classList.add('show');
}
document.getElementById('againBtn').addEventListener('click', (e)=>{ e.stopPropagation(); startGame(); });

// ---- input ----
window.addEventListener('keydown', (e)=>{
  const k = e.key.toLowerCase();
  if([' ','arrowup','arrowdown','arrowleft','arrowright'].includes(e.key.toLowerCase())) e.preventDefault();
  if(mode==='title' || mode==='gameover'){
    if(k===' '||k==='enter'||k==='w'||k==='arrowup') startGame();
    return;
  }
  if(mode!=='playing') return;
  if(k==='arrowup'||k==='w') hop(0,1);
  else if(k==='arrowdown'||k==='s') hop(0,-1);
  else if(k==='arrowleft'||k==='a') hop(-1,0);
  else if(k==='arrowright'||k==='d') hop(1,0);
});

const stage = document.getElementById('stage');
let sx0=0, sy0=0, down=false;
stage.addEventListener('pointerdown', (e)=>{
  down = true; sx0 = e.clientX; sy0 = e.clientY;
});
stage.addEventListener('pointerup', (e)=>{
  if(!down) return; down=false;
  if(overScreen.classList.contains('show')) return; // button handles it
  const dx = e.clientX-sx0, dy = e.clientY-sy0;
  if(mode==='title' || mode==='gameover'){ startGame(); return; }
  if(mode!=='playing') return;
  const ax=Math.abs(dx), ay=Math.abs(dy);
  if(ax<18 && ay<18){ hop(0,1); }
  else if(ax>ay){ hop(dx>0?1:-1, 0); }
  else { hop(0, dy<0?1:-1); }
});
stage.addEventListener('pointercancel', ()=>{ down=false; });

// ---- boot ----
initWorld();
initClouds();
mode = 'title';
requestAnimationFrame(loop);
})();
</script>
</body>
</html>
```

```html
<script>
(function(){
"use strict";

// ---------- canvas setup ----------
const canvas = document.getElementById('game');
const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
let DPR = Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 2);
let W = 0, H = 0;

function resize(){
  W = window.innerWidth; H = window.innerHeight;
  canvas.width = Math.floor(W * DPR);
  canvas.height = Math.floor(H * DPR);
  canvas.style.width = W + 'px';
  canvas.style.height = H + 'px';
}
window.addEventListener('resize', resize);
resize();

// ---------- constants ----------
const TILE_W = 64, TILE_H = 32, TILE_DEPTH = 16;
const GRID_MIN = -7, GRID_MAX = 7;
const BEHIND_ROWS = 6, AHEAD_ROWS = 15;
const HOP_DURATION = 0.13;

const CAR_COLORS = ['#ff6b6b','#4ecdc4','#ffd93d','#a78bfa','#ff9f5c','#5cd3ff'];
const TRUCK_COLORS = ['#e0e0e0','#8a94a6','#ffb84c'];

function rand(a,b){ return a + Math.random()*(b-a); }
function pick(arr){ return arr[Math.floor(Math.random()*arr.length)]; }
function clamp(v,a,b){ return Math.max(a, Math.min(b,v)); }
function lerp(a,b,t){ return a + (b-a)*t; }
function easeOutQuad(t){ return 1 - (1-t)*(1-t); }

// ---------- state ----------
let state = 'title'; // title | playing | gameover
let time = 0;

let best = 0;
try { best = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('voxelHopBest') || '0', 10) || 0; } catch(e){ best = 0; }

let score = 0;
let coinBonus = 0;
let coinsCollected = 0;
let maxRowReached = 0;

const lanes = new Map();
let lastLaneTypes = [];

let camera = { x: 0, y: 0 };
let shake = { x: 0, y: 0, t: 0, mag: 0 };

let particles = [];

const player = {
  col: 0, row: 0,
  startCol: 0, startRow: 0,
  targetCol: 0, targetRow: 0,
  hopT: 1, isHopping: false,
  facing: 'up', dead: false, deathTimer: 0,
  onLog: false, currentLog: null, rideOffset: 0,
  squash: 0
};

let hintShown = false;
let hintTimer = 0;

// ---------- lane generation ----------
function generateLane(row){
  let type;
  if(row <= 1){
    type = 'grass';
  } else {
    const diff = clamp((row - 2) / 140, 0, 1);
    const weights = {
      grass: 0.34,
      road: 0.27 + diff*0.08,
      river: 0.22 + diff*0.04,
      rail: 0.09 + diff*0.10
    };
    const prevA = lastLaneTypes[lastLaneTypes.length-1];
    const prevB = lastLaneTypes[lastLaneTypes.length-2];
    if(prevA && prevA !== 'grass' && prevB && prevB !== 'grass'){
      type = 'grass';
    } else {
      // avoid rails too close together
      let recentRail = lastLaneTypes.slice(-3).includes('rail');
      let pool = [];
      for(const k in weights){
        if(k === 'rail' && recentRail) continue;
        pool.push([k, weights[k]]);
      }
      const total = pool.reduce((s,p)=>s+p[1],0);
      let r = Math.random()*total;
      type = pool[0][0];
      for(const [k,w] of pool){ if(r < w){ type = k; break;} r -= w; }
    }
  }

  lastLaneTypes.push(type);
  if(lastLaneTypes.length > 6) lastLaneTypes.shift();

  const diff = clamp((row - 2) / 140, 0, 1);
  const lane = { row, type, coins: [] };

  if(type === 'grass'){
    const n = Math.random() < 0.55 ? (Math.random()<0.3?2:1) : 0;
    const cols = [];
    for(let i=0;i<GRID_MAX-GRID_MIN+1;i++) cols.push(GRID_MIN+i);
    for(let i=0;i<n;i++){
      const c = pick(cols);
      if(!lane.coins.find(co=>co.col===c)) lane.coins.push({ col: c, collected: false, seed: Math.random()*10 });
    }
    lane.decor = Math.random() < 0.4;
  }

  if(type === 'road'){
    lane.dir = Math.random() < 0.5 ? 1 : -1;
    lane.speed = 1.6 + diff*2.2;
    const count = 3 + Math.floor(Math.random()*2);
    const span = GRID_MAX - GRID_MIN + 1;
    const gap = span / count;
    lane.vehicles = [];
    for(let i=0;i<count;i++){
      const isTruck = Math.random() < 0.25;
      lane.vehicles.push({
        col: GRID_MIN + i*gap + Math.random()*gap*0.6,
        width: isTruck ? 2 : 1,
        speed: lane.speed * (0.85 + Math.random()*0.3),
        color: pick(isTruck ? TRUCK_COLORS : CAR_COLORS),
        isTruck
      });
    }
  }

  if(type === 'river'){
    lane.dir = Math.random() < 0.5 ? 1 : -1;
    lane.speed = 1.0 + diff*1.3;
    const logs = [];
    let c = GRID_MIN - Math.random()*2;
    while(c < GRID_MAX + 2){
      const len = 2 + Math.floor(Math.random()*2);
      logs.push({ col: c + len/2, len, vx: 0 });
      c += len + 1.4 + Math.random()*1.6;
    }
    lane.logs = logs;
  }

  if(type === 'rail'){
    lane.cycle = Math.max(3.6, 6.2 - diff*2.2);
    lane.warnDur = 1.0;
    lane.activeDur = 0.55;
    lane.phase = Math.random() * lane.cycle;
    lane.trainDir = Math.random() < 0.5 ? 1 : -1;
    lane.state = 'idle';
    lane.train = null;
  }

  lanes.set(row, lane);
  return lane;
}

function getLane(row){
  let l = lanes.get(row);
  if(!l) l = generateLane(row);
  return l;
}

function ensureLanesGenerated(){
  const from = maxRowReached - BEHIND_ROWS;
  const to = maxRowReached + AHEAD_ROWS;
  for(let r = from; r <= to; r++){
    if(!lanes.has(r)) generateLane(r);
  }
}

function pruneLanes(){
  const cutoff = maxRowReached - BEHIND_ROWS - 3;
  for(const key of lanes.keys()){
    if(key < cutoff) lanes.delete(key);
  }
}

// ---------- lane update ----------
function updateLane(lane, dt){
  if(lane.type === 'road'){
    for(const v of lane.vehicles){
      v.col += lane.dir * v.speed * dt;
      if(lane.dir > 0 && v.col > GRID_MAX + 3) v.col = GRID_MIN - 3 - Math.random()*3;
      if(lane.dir < 0 && v.col < GRID_MIN - 3) v.col = GRID_MAX + 3 + Math.random()*3;
    }
  } else if(lane.type === 'river'){
    for(const log of lane.logs){
      log.vx = lane.dir * lane.speed;
      log.col += log.vx * dt;
      const span = GRID_MAX - GRID_MIN + 4;
      if(lane.dir > 0 && log.col - log.len/2 > GRID_MAX + 3) log.col -= span + log.len;
      if(lane.dir < 0 && log.col + log.len/2 < GRID_MIN - 3) log.col += span + log.len;
    }
  } else if(lane.type === 'rail'){
    lane.phase += dt;
    const idleDur = lane.cycle - lane.warnDur - lane.activeDur;
    if(lane.state === 'idle' && lane.phase > idleDur){
      lane.state = 'warning'; lane.phase = 0;
    } else if(lane.state === 'warning' && lane.phase > lane.warnDur){
      lane.state = 'active'; lane.phase = 0;
      const startCol = lane.trainDir > 0 ? GRID_MIN - 4 : GRID_MAX + 4;
      lane.train = { col: startCol, speed: (GRID_MAX-GRID_MIN+8) / lane.activeDur };
    } else if(lane.state === 'active'){
      lane.train.col += lane.trainDir * lane.train.speed * dt;
      if(lane.phase > lane.activeDur){
        lane.state = 'idle'; lane.phase = 0; lane.train = null;
      }
    }
  }
}

// ---------- player movement ----------
function tryMove(dc, dr){
  if(state !== 'playing' || player.isHopping || player.dead) return;
  const curCol = Math.round(player.col);
  const curRow = Math.round(player.row);
  const nc = curCol + dc, nr = curRow + dr;
  if(nc < GRID_MIN || nc > GRID_MAX) return;
  if(nr < maxRowReached - BEHIND_ROWS + 2) return;

  getLane(nr);

  player.startCol = player.col; player.startRow = player.row;
  player.targetCol = nc; player.targetRow = nr;
  player.hopT = 0; player.isHopping = true;
  player.onLog = false; player.currentLog = null;
  if(dc > 0) player.facing = 'right';
  else if(dc < 0) player.facing = 'left';
  else if(dr > 0) player.facing = 'up';
  else if(dr < 0) player.facing = 'down';

  hintTimer = 999; // hide hint once player moves
}

function collectCoinAt(row, col){
  const lane = getLane(row);
  if(!lane.coins) return;
  for(const c of lane.coins){
    if(!c.collected && c.col === col){
      c.collected = true;
      coinsCollected++;
      coinBonus += 5;
      updateScore();
      spawnSparkle(col, row);
      spawnFloatText(col, row, '+5');
    }
  }
}

function updateScore(){
  score = maxRowReached + coinBonus;
}

function landOnLane(){
  const row = player.targetRow;
  const col = player.targetCol;
  const lane = getLane(row);

  if(row > maxRowReached){ maxRowReached = row; }
  updateScore();

  if(lane.type === 'river'){
    let found = null;
    for(const log of lane.logs){
      if(col >= log.col - log.len/2 - 0.15 && col <= log.col + log.len/2 + 0.15){ found = log; break; }
    }
    if(found){
      player.onLog = true;
      player.currentLog = found;
      player.rideOffset = player.col - found.col;
    } else {
      die('water');
      return;
    }
  } else if(lane.type === 'road'){
    for(const v of lane.vehicles){
      if(col >= v.col - v.width/2 - 0.05 && col <= v.col + v.width/2 + 0.05){ die('vehicle'); return; }
    }
  } else if(lane.type === 'rail'){
    if(lane.state === 'active'){ die('train'); return; }
  }

  if(lane.type === 'grass'){
    collectCoinAt(row, col);
  }
}

function continuousChecks(dt){
  const row = Math.round(player.row);
  const lane = getLane(row);

  if(lane.type === 'river' && player.onLog && player.currentLog){
    player.col = player.currentLog.col + player.rideOffset;
    if(player.col < GRID_MIN - 1 || player.col > GRID_MAX + 1){ die('water'); return; }
  } else if(lane.type === 'river' && !player.onLog){
    die('water'); return;
  }

  if(lane.type === 'road'){
    const col = player.col;
    for(const v of lane.vehicles){
      if(col >= v.col - v.width/2 - 0.05 && col <= v.col + v.width/2 + 0.05){ die('vehicle'); return; }
    }
  }

  if(lane.type === 'rail' && lane.state === 'active'){
    die('train'); return;
  }
}

function updatePlayerHop(dt){
  if(!player.isHopping) return;
  player.hopT += dt / HOP_DURATION;
  if(player.hopT >= 1){
    player.hopT = 1;
    player.col = player.targetCol;
    player.row = player.targetRow;
    player.isHopping = false;
    landOnLane();
  }
}

function die(reason){
  if(player.dead) return;
  player.dead = true;
  player.deathTimer = 0.85;
  triggerShake(reason === 'train' ? 14 : 9);
  spawnDeathBurst(player.col, player.row, reason);
}

function finalizeGameOver(){
  if(score > best){
    best = score;
    try { localStorage.setItem('voxelHopBest', String(best)); } catch(e){}
    document.getElementById('newBestBadge').style.display = 'inline-block';
  } else {
    document.getElementById('newBestBadge').style.display = 'none';
  }
  document.getElementById('finalScore').textContent = score;
  document.getElementById('bestScore').textContent = best;
  state = 'gameover';
  document.getElementById('gameOverScreen').classList.remove('hidden');
}

// ---------- particles ----------
function spawnSparkle(col, row){
  for(let i=0;i<10;i++){
    const ang = Math.random()*Math.PI*2;
    const spd = rand(0.8, 2.2);
    particles.push({
      type:'spark', col, row, life: rand(0.35,0.6), maxLife: 0.6,
      vx: Math.cos(ang)*spd, vy: Math.sin(ang)*spd - 1.2,
      z: 0, vz: rand(1.5,3),
      color: pick(['#ffd93d','#ffe98a','#fff2b0']),
      size: rand(3,5)
    });
  }
}

function spawnFloatText(col, row, text){
  particles.push({ type:'text', col, row, text, life: 0.9, maxLife: 0.9, z: 8, vz: 14 });
}

function spawnDeathBurst(col, row, reason){
  const color = reason === 'water' ? '#5cc9ff' : (reason === 'train' ? '#ffdd55' : '#ff6b6b');
  for(let i=0;i<22;i++){
    const ang = Math.random()*Math.PI*2;
    const spd = rand(1.5, 4.5);
    particles.push({
      type:'cube', col, row, life: rand(0.5,0.9), maxLife: 0.9,
      vx: Math.cos(ang)*spd, vy: Math.sin(ang)*spd,
      z: rand(4,10), vz: rand(4,9), gravity: -14,
      color, size: rand(4,8), rot: Math.random()*Math.PI
    });
  }
}

function updateParticles(dt){
  for(let i=particles.length-1;i>=0;i--){
    const p = particles[i];
    p.life -= dt;
    if(p.life <= 0){ particles.splice(i,1); continue; }
    p.col += (p.vx||0)*dt;
    p.row += (p.vy||0)*dt;
    if(p.gravity){
      p.vz += p.gravity*dt;
      p.z += p.vz*dt;
      if(p.z < 0){ p.z = 0; p.vz *= -0.35; }
    } else if(p.type === 'text'){
      p.z += (p.vz||0)*dt;
      p.vz *= 0.96;
    } else if(p.type === 'spark'){
      p.z += (p.vz||0)*dt;
      p.vz -= 6*dt;
    }
  }
}

function triggerShake(mag){
  shake.mag = mag; shake.t = 0.35;
}
function updateShake(dt){
  if(shake.t > 0){
    shake.t -= dt;
    const m = shake.mag * (shake.t/0.35);
    shake.x = (Math.random()-0.5)*m;
    shake.y = (Math.random()-0.5)*m;
    if(shake.t <= 0){ shake.x = 0; shake.y = 0; }
  }
}

// ---------- camera ----------
function worldToScreen(col, row){
  return {
    x: (col - row) * (TILE_W/2),
    y: (col + row) * (TILE_H/2)
  };
}

function updateCamera(dt){
  const target = worldToScreen(player.col, player.row);
  camera.x = lerp(camera.x, target.x, Math.min(1, dt*6));
  camera.y = lerp(camera.y, target.y, Math.min(1, dt*6));
}

// ---------- reset / start ----------
function resetGame(){
  lanes.clear();
  lastLaneTypes = [];
  particles = [];
  score = 0; coinBonus = 0; coinsCollected = 0; maxRowReached = 0;
  player.col = 0; player.row = 0;
  player.startCol = 0; player.startRow = 0;
  player.targetCol = 0; player.targetRow = 0;
  player.hopT = 1; player.isHopping = false;
  player.dead = false; player.deathTimer = 0;
  player.onLog = false; player.currentLog = null;
  player.facing = 'up';
  camera.x = 0; camera.y = 0;
  shake = { x:0, y:0, t:0, mag:0 };
  hintTimer = 0; hintShown = false;
  for(let r=-BEHIND_ROWS-2; r<=2; r++) generateLane(r);
  ensureLanesGenerated();
}

function startGame(){
  resetGame();
  state = 'playing';
  document.getElementById('titleScreen').classList.add('hidden');
  document.getElementById('gameOverScreen').classList.add('hidden');
}

// ---------- rendering ----------
const skyGrad_cache = {};
function drawSky(){
  const g = ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,0,H);
  g.addColorStop(0, '#ff9d76');
  g.addColorStop(0.35, '#ffb0a3');
  g.addColorStop(0.6, '#c9a3e0');
  g.addColorStop(1, '#3b3d8f');
  ctx.fillStyle = g;
  ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);

  // clouds with slight parallax
  ctx.save();
  const offset = -(camera.x * 0.05) % 400;
  for(let i=-1;i<4;i++){
    for(let j=0;j<3;j++){
      const cx = ((i*400 + j*130 + offset) % (W+400)) - 200;
      const cy = 60 + j*70 + Math.sin(time*0.3 + j)*6;
      drawCloud(cx, cy, 46 + j*10);
    }
  }
  ctx.restore();
}

function drawCloud(x,y,s){
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.55)';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(x, y, s, s*0.45, 0, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.ellipse(x+s*0.6, y+4, s*0.65, s*0.35, 0, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.ellipse(x-s*0.6, y+6, s*0.55, s*0.3, 0, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fill();
}

function drawVoxelBlock(cx, cy, topColor, sideL, sideR, height){
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(cx, cy - TILE_H/2);
  ctx.lineTo(cx + TILE_W/2, cy);
  ctx.lineTo(cx, cy + TILE_H/2);
  ctx.lineTo(cx - TILE_W/2, cy);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.fillStyle = topColor;
  ctx.fill();

  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(cx - TILE_W/2, cy);
  ctx.lineTo(cx, cy + TILE_H/2);
  ctx.lineTo(cx, cy + TILE_H/2 + height);
  ctx.lineTo(cx - TILE_W/2, cy + height);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.fillStyle = sideL;
  ctx.fill();

  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(cx + TILE_W/2, cy);
  ctx.lineTo(cx, cy + TILE_H/2);
  ctx.lineTo(cx, cy + TILE_H/2 + height);
  ctx.lineTo(cx + TILE_W/2, cy + height);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.fillStyle = sideR;
  ctx.fill();
}

function shadeColor(hex, amt){
  const c = parseInt(hex.slice(1),16);
  let r = (c>>16)&255, g=(c>>8)&255, b=c&255;
  r = clamp(Math.round(r+amt),0,255); g = clamp(Math.round(g+amt),0,255); b = clamp(Math.round(b+amt),0,255);
  return `rgb(${r},${g},${b})`;
}

function laneTopColors(lane, col){
  const checker = (lane.row + col) % 2 === 0;
  if(lane.type === 'grass'){
    return checker ? '#7ed957' : '#6bc848';
  }
  if(lane.type === 'road'){
    return '#3b3f4a';
  }
  if(lane.type === 'river'){
    const shimmer = Math.sin(time*2 + col*0.6 + lane.row*0.4) * 8;
    const base = checker ? [64,168,222] : [58,158,214];
    return `rgb(${base[0]},${base[1]+shimmer},${base[2]})`;
  }
  if(lane.type === 'rail'){
    return checker ? '#8a6b4a' : '#7d5f42';
  }
  return '#888';
}

function drawTile(col, row, lane){
  const p = worldToScreen(col, row);
  const top = laneTopColors(lane, col);
  let depth = TILE_DEPTH;
  if(lane.type === 'river') depth = TILE_DEPTH * 0.6;
  drawVoxelBlock(p.x, p.y, top, shadeColor(top,-40), shadeColor(top,-70), depth);

  if(lane.type === 'road'){
    // lane dashes along direction of travel
    if(((col - Math.floor(time*2)*0 + Math.round(lane.row))% 2 === 0)){
      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.55)';
      ctx.fillRect(p.x-3, p.y-2, 6, 4);
    }
  }
  if(lane.type === 'rail'){
    ctx.strokeStyle = '#2b2b2b';
    ctx.lineWidth = 3;
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(p.x - TILE_W/2 + 6, p.y - 3);
    ctx.lineTo(p.x + TILE_W/2 - 6, p.y + 3);
    ctx.stroke();
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(p.x - TILE_W/2 + 6, p.y + 5);
    ctx.lineTo(p.x + TILE_W/2 - 6, p.y + 11);
    ctx.stroke();
    if(lane.state === 'warning'){
      const blink = Math.sin(time*18) > 0;
      if(blink){
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,60,60,0.85)';
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(p.x, p.y - 14, 4, 0, Math.PI*2);
        ctx.fill();
      }
    }
  }
}

function drawCoin(col, row, coin){
  if(coin.collected) return;
  const p = worldToScreen(col, row);
  const bob = Math.sin(time*4 + coin.seed) * 3;
  const scaleX = Math.abs(Math.cos(time*2.2 + coin.seed));
  ctx.save();
  ctx.translate(p.x, p.y - 14 - bob);
  ctx.scale(Math.max(0.25,scaleX), 1);
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.arc(0,0, 8, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fillStyle = '#ffd93d';
  ctx.fill();
  ctx.lineWidth = 2;
  ctx.strokeStyle = '#e8a900';
  ctx.stroke();
  ctx.restore();
}

function drawVehicle(v, lane){
  const p = worldToScreen(v.col, lane.row);
  const w = v.width * TILE_W * 0.42;
  const h = TILE_H * 0.7;
  const top = v.color;
  ctx.save();
  ctx.translate(p.x, p.y - 6);
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(-w, -h*0.5);
  ctx.lineTo(w, -h*0.5);
  ctx.lineTo(w*0.8, h*0.5);
  ctx.lineTo(-w*0.8, h*0.5);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.fillStyle = top;
  ctx.fill();
  ctx.fillStyle = shadeColor(top, -50);
  ctx.fillRect(-w*0.8, h*0.5-2, w*1.6, 10);
  // cabin
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(230,245,255,0.75)';
  ctx.fillRect(-w*0.4, -h*0.35, w*0.8, h*0.4);
  ctx.restore();
}

function drawLog(log, lane){
  const p = worldToScreen(log.col, lane.row);
  const w = log.len * TILE_W * 0.5;
  ctx.save();
  ctx.translate(p.x, p.y);
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(0, 4, w*0.52, TILE_H*0.42, 0, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fillStyle = '#8a5a2c';
  ctx.fill();
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(0, 0, w*0.5, TILE_H*0.38, 0, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fillStyle = '#a8703c';
  ctx.fill();
  ctx.strokeStyle = '#7a4d24';
  ctx.lineWidth = 2;
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(0,0,w*0.5,TILE_H*0.38,0,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.stroke();
  ctx.restore();
}

function drawTrain(lane){
  if(!lane.train) return;
  const p = worldToScreen(lane.train.col, lane.row);
  ctx.save();
  ctx.translate(p.x, p.y - 10);
  ctx.fillStyle = '#3a4a6b';
  ctx.fillRect(-TILE_W*1.4, -18, TILE_W*2.8, 34);
  ctx.fillStyle = '#ffdd55';
  for(let i=-1;i<=1;i++){
    ctx.fillRect(i*TILE_W*0.7 - 6, -6, 12, 10);
  }
  ctx.restore();
}

function drawPlayer(){
  const dc = player.isHopping ? lerp(player.startCol, player.targetCol, easeOutQuad(player.hopT)) : player.col;
  const dr = player.isHopping ? lerp(player.startRow, player.targetRow, easeOutQuad(player.hopT)) : player.row;
  const p = worldToScreen(dc, dr);

  const arc = player.isHopping ? Math.sin(player.hopT * Math.PI) : 0;
  const hopHeight = arc * 22;
  let squashY = 1, squashX = 1;
  if(player.isHopping){
    squashY = 1 - Math.sin(player.hopT*Math.PI)*0.18 + 0.0;
    squashX = 1 + Math.sin(player.hopT*Math.PI)*0.12;
    if(player.hopT < 0.12) { squashY = 0.7; squashX = 1.25; }
  } else if(player.dead){
    squashY = 0.5; squashX = 1.4;
  }

  const flip = player.facing === 'left' ? -1 : 1;

  ctx.save();
  ctx.translate(p.x, p.y - hopHeight - 4);
  ctx.scale(flip, 1);

  // shadow
  ctx.save();
  ctx.globalAlpha = 0.3 * (1 - arc*0.6);
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(0, hopHeight + 8, 16*(1-arc*0.3), 7*(1-arc*0.3), 0, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fillStyle = '#000';
  ctx.fill();
  ctx.restore();

  ctx.scale(squashX, squashY);

  if(player.dead){
    ctx.globalAlpha = Math.max(0, player.deathTimer / 0.85);
  }

  // body
  ctx.fillStyle = '#ff6b7a';
  roundRect(-13, -24, 26, 24, 7);
  ctx.fill();
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.15)';
  roundRect(-13, -6, 26, 6, 3); ctx.fill();

  // head
  ctx.fillStyle = '#ffd27b';
  roundRect(-11, -42, 22, 20, 7);
  ctx.fill();

  // eyes
  ctx.fillStyle = '#2a1830';
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(-4, -33, 2.4, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(5, -33, 2.4, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();

  ctx.restore();
}

function roundRect(x,y,w,h,r){
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(x+r,y);
  ctx.arcTo(x+w,y,x+w,y+h,r);
  ctx.arcTo(x+w,y+h,x,y+h,r);
  ctx.arcTo(x,y+h,x,y,r);
  ctx.arcTo(x,y,x+w,y,r);
  ctx.closePath();
}

function drawParticle(pt){
  const p = worldToScreen(pt.col, pt.row);
  const alpha = clamp(pt.life / pt.maxLife, 0, 1);
  ctx.save();
  ctx.globalAlpha = alpha;
  if(pt.type === 'cube'){
    ctx.translate(p.x, p.y - pt.z);
    ctx.rotate(pt.rot);
    ctx.fillStyle = pt.color;
    ctx.fillRect(-pt.size/2, -pt.size/2, pt.size, pt.size);
  } else if(pt.type === 'spark'){
    ctx.translate(p.x, p.y - 14 - pt.z);
    ctx.fillStyle = pt.color;
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.arc(0,0,pt.size*alpha,0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fill();
  } else if(pt.type === 'text'){
    ctx.translate(p.x, p.y - 14 - pt.z);
    ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(255,217,61,${alpha})`;
    ctx.font = '800 16px -apple-system, sans-serif';
    ctx.textAlign = 'center';
    ctx.fillText(pt.text, 0, 0);
  }
  ctx.restore();
}

function render(){
  ctx.setTransform(DPR,0,0,DPR,0,0);
  ctx.clearRect(0,0,W,H);
  drawSky();

  const zoom = clamp(Math.min(W,900)/760, 0.62, 1.05);

  ctx.save();
  ctx.translate(W/2, H*0.52);
  ctx.scale(zoom, zoom);
  ctx.translate(-camera.x + shake.x, -camera.y + shake.y);

  // build painter's-sorted render list
  const list = [];
  const centerRow = Math.round(player.row);
  const rowFrom = centerRow - BEHIND_ROWS, rowTo = centerRow + AHEAD_ROWS;

  for(let r = rowFrom; r <= rowTo; r++){
    const lane = lanes.get(r);
    if(!lane) continue;
    for(let c = GRID_MIN; c <= GRID_MAX; c++){
      const key = c + r;
      list.push({ key: key - 0.5, draw: (function(cc,rr,ln){ return ()=>drawTile(cc,rr,ln); })(c,r,lane) });
    }
    if(lane.coins){
      for(const coin of lane.coins){
        if(!coin.collected) list.push({ key: coin.col + r + 0.05, draw: ()=>drawCoin(coin.col, r, coin) });
      }
    }
    if(lane.type === 'road'){
      for(const v of lane.vehicles){
        list.push({ key: v.col + r + 0.1, draw: (function(vv,ln){ return ()=>drawVehicle(vv,ln); })(v,lane) });
      }
    }
    if(lane.type === 'river'){
      for(const log of lane.logs){
        list.push({ key: log.col + r + 0.1, draw: (function(lg,ln){ return ()=>drawLog(lg,ln); })(log,lane) });
      }
    }
    if(lane.type === 'rail' && lane.state === 'active' && lane.train){
      list.push({ key: lane.train.col + r + 0.15, draw: ()=>drawTrain(lane) });
    }
  }

  const pdc = player.isHopping ? lerp(player.startCol, player.targetCol, player.hopT) : player.col;
  const pdr = player.isHopping ? lerp(player.startRow, player.targetRow, player.hopT) : player.row;
  list.push({ key: pdc + pdr + 0.2, draw: drawPlayer });

  for(const pt of particles){
    list.push({ key: pt.col + pt.row + 0.3, draw: (function(p){ return ()=>drawParticle(p); })(pt) });
  }

  list.sort((a,b)=>a.key-b.key);
  for(const item of list) item.draw();

  ctx.restore();

  drawHUD();
}

function drawHUD(){
  if(state !== 'playing' && state !== 'gameover') return;
  // score pill
  ctx.save();
  const pillW = 150, pillH = 44;
  const px = 16, py = 16;
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(20,10,35,0.55)';
  roundRect(px, py, pillW, pillH, 22); ctx.fill();
  ctx.fillStyle = '#ffe98a';
  ctx.font = '800 22px -apple-system, sans-serif';
  ctx.textAlign = 'left'; ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
  ctx.fillText(String(score), px+18, py+pillH/2);
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.6)';
  ctx.font = '600 11px -apple-system, sans-serif';
  ctx.fillText('SCORE  ·  BEST ' + best, px+18, py+pillH/2+16);
  ctx.restore();

  // coin counter
  ctx.save();
  const cw = 96, ch = 40;
  const cx = W - cw - 16, cy = 16;
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(20,10,35,0.55)';
  roundRect(cx, cy, cw, ch, 20); ctx.fill();
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.arc(cx+22, cy+ch/2, 10, 0, Math.PI*2);
  ctx.fillStyle = '#ffd93d'; ctx.fill();
  ctx.strokeStyle = '#e8a900'; ctx.lineWidth = 2; ctx.stroke();
  ctx.fillStyle = '#fff';
  ctx.font = '800 18px -apple-system, sans-serif';
  ctx.textAlign = 'left'; ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
  ctx.fillText(String(coinsCollected), cx+40, cy+ch/2+1);
  ctx.restore();
}

// ---------- main loop ----------
let lastT = performance.now();
function frame(now){
  const dt = Math.min((now - lastT)/1000, 0.05);
  lastT = now;

  if(state === 'playing'){
    time += dt;
    updateCamera(dt);
    ensureLanesGenerated();
    pruneLanes();
    const centerRow = Math.round(player.row);
    for(let r = centerRow - BEHIND_ROWS; r <= centerRow + AHEAD_ROWS; r++){
      const lane = lanes.get(r);
      if(lane) updateLane(lane, dt);
    }
    updatePlayerHop(dt);
    if(!player.isHopping && !player.dead) continuousChecks(dt);
    updateParticles(dt);
    updateShake(dt);

    if(player.dead){
      player.deathTimer -= dt;
      if(player.deathTimer <= 0) finalizeGameOver();
    }

    hintTimer += dt;
    const hintEl = document.getElementById('swipeHint');
    if(hintTimer > 0.6 && hintTimer < 4 && !player.dead){
      hintEl.classList.add('show');
    } else {
      hintEl.classList.remove('show');
    }
  } else if(state === 'title'){
    time += dt;
  } else if(state === 'gameover'){
    updateParticles(dt);
    updateShake(dt);
  }

  render();
  requestAnimationFrame(frame);
}
requestAnimationFrame(frame);

// ---------- input ----------
window.addEventListener('keydown', (e)=>{
  if(e.code === 'Space'){
    if(state === 'title'){ startGame(); e.preventDefault(); return; }
    if(state === 'gameover'){ startGame(); e.preventDefault(); return; }
  }
  if(state !== 'playing' || e.repeat) return;
  switch(e.code){
    case 'ArrowUp': case 'KeyW': tryMove(0, 1); break;
    case 'ArrowDown': case 'KeyS': tryMove(0, -1); break;
    case 'ArrowLeft': case 'KeyA': tryMove(-1, 0); break;
    case 'ArrowRight': case 'KeyD': tryMove(1, 0); break;
  }
});

document.getElementById('playBtn').addEventListener('click', startGame);
document.getElementById('retryBtn').addEventListener('click', startGame);

let touchStart = null;
canvas.addEventListener('touchstart', (e)=>{
  const t = e.changedTouches[0];
  touchStart = { x: t.clientX, y: t.clientY, time: performance.now() };
}, {passive:true});

canvas.addEventListener('touchend', (e)=>{
  if(state === 'title'){ startGame(); return; }
  if(!touchStart) return;
  const t = e.changedTouches[0];
  const dx = t.clientX - touchStart.x;
  const dy = t.clientY - touchStart.y;
  const dt = performance.now() - touchStart.time;
  const dist = Math.hypot(dx,dy);

  if(state !== 'playing'){ touchStart = null; return; }

  if(dist < 24 && dt < 300){
    tryMove(0, 1); // tap = forward hop
  } else if(dist >= 24){
    if(Math.abs(dx) > Math.abs(dy)){
      tryMove(dx > 0 ? 1 : -1, 0);
    } else {
      tryMove(0, dy > 0 ? -1 : 1);
    }
  }
  touchStart = null;
}, {passive:true});

canvas.addEventListener('click', ()=>{
  if(state === 'title') startGame();
});

// ---------- init ----------
resetGame();
render();

})();
</script>
</body>
</html>
```
