            box-shadow: 0 8px 20px rgba(255, 100, 145, 0.7);

             margin-top: 20px;

<body>

<div id="gameContainer">
    <canvas id="gameCanvas"></canvas>

    <!-- UI Overlays -->
    <div id="uiOverlay">
        <div class="ui-pill" id="scoreDisplay">Score: 0</div>
        <div class="ui-pill" id="coinCounter">💰: 0</div>
    </div>

    <!-- Start Screen Overlay -->
    <div id="startScreen" class="game-screen" style="pointer-events: auto;">
        <h1 id="titleLogo">VOXEL HOP</h1>
        <p>A colorful, endless voxel journey.</p>
        <button class="btn-play" onclick="startGame()">Press Space or Tap to Play</button>
        <div id="message">High Score: 0</div>
    </div>

    <!-- Game Over Screen Overlay -->
    <div id="gameOverScreen" class="game-screen" style="display: none; pointer-events: auto;">
        <h2>GAME OVER</h2>
        <p>You crashed!</p>
        <h3 id="finalScore">Your Score: 0</h3>
        <h3 id="bestScoreDisplay">Best Score: 0</h3>
        <button class="btn-play" onclick="resetGame()">Play Again</button>
    </div>

<script>
// --- CONSTANTS AND INITIALIZATION ---

const CANVAS_WIDTH = 500; // Matches CSS container width
const CANVAS_HEIGHT = 900; // Fixed height for better vertical scrolling visual
const TILE_SIZE = 50; // Defines the size of one voxel unit (both X and Y)

// Canvas setup
const canvas = document.getElementById('gameCanvas');
canvas.width = CANVAS_WIDTH;
canvas.height = CANVAS_HEIGHT;
const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');

// Game State Variables
let gameRunning = false;
let lastTime = 0;
const GRAVITY_SCROLL_SPEED = 1.5; // Determines how fast the world scrolls up when playing

// Player state
let player = {
    x: CANVAS_WIDTH / 2,
    y: canvas.height - (TILE_SIZE * 3), // Start near the bottom
    size: TILE_SIZE * 0.8,
    dy: 0,
    speed: 5, // Movement speed per hop
    isJumping: false,
    currentTileY: Math.floor((canvas.height - (TILE_SIZE * 3)) / TILE_SIZE)
};

// Game state trackers
let gameState = {
    score: 0,
    coins: 0,
    bestScore: parseInt(localStorage.getItem('voxelHopBestScore') || '0'),
    difficultyTimer: 0,
    gameSpeedMultiplier: 1.0
};

// World generation parameters
const LANE_GENERATION_COUNT = 25; // How many rows ahead of the player to generate
let lanes = [];

// Particle and collision systems
let particles = {
    coinTrail: [],
    deathBurst: []
};
let screenShakeTimer = 0;

// Helper object for tracking moving objects (cars, trains)
const movers = {
    roads: [],
    trains: [],
    time: 0 // Global tick counter
};


// --- UTILITY & MATH FUNCTIONS ---

/** Simple bounding box check */
function isColliding(x1, y1, w1, h1, x2, y2, w2, h2) {
    return (
        x1 < x2 + w2 &&
        x1 + w1 > x2 &&
        y1 < y2 + h2 &&
        y1 + h1 > y2
    );
}

/** Random integer helper */
function randInt(min, max) {
    return Math.floor(Math.random() * (max - min + 1)) + min;
}

// --- LANE STRUCTURES ---

class Lane {
    constructor(yIndex, type, details = {}) {
        this.yIndex = yIndex; // Vertical grid index (0 is top)
        this.type = type;
        this.details = details;
        this.xOffset = randInt(0, CANVAS_WIDTH - TILE_SIZE); // Horizontal position start
    }

    // Checks if a given tile (x, y) within this lane is safe for the player's hitbox
    isSafe(px, py, pw, ph) {
        const relativeY = Math.min(py, canvas.height - 50); // Assume player Y is normalized to grid scale

        if (this.type === 'Grass') return true;
        if (this.type === 'Road' || this.type === 'Railroad') {
            // For now, collision checks are handled globally per frame
            return true; 
        }
        if (this.type === 'River') {
            // Example: Only safe if player is exactly at the coordinates of a log/raft detail
            const raftPresent = this.details.logs && Math.random() < 0.5; // Simplified check
            return raftPresent || false;
        }
        return true; // Default safety assumption for newly generated lanes
    }

    draw(y) {
        const topY = y * TILE_SIZE;

        ctx.save();
        ctx.translate(0, topY); // Move drawing context to the top of this lane

        switch (this.type) {
            case 'Grass':
                // Grass: Green voxel look
                ctx.fillStyle = '#4caf50';
                ctx.shadowColor = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2)';
                ctx.shadowBlur = 10;
                ctx.fillRect(0, 0, CANVAS_WIDTH, TILE_SIZE);
                break;

            case 'Road':
                // Road: Asphalt look with curb details
                const roadColor = '#444';
                ctx.fillStyle = roadColor;
                ctx.shadowBlur = 15;
                ctx.fillRect(0, 0, CANVAS_WIDTH, TILE_SIZE);

                // Draw Curb (Fake depth/detail)
                ctx.fillStyle = '#8b4513'; // Brown curb color
                ctx.fillRect(0, TILE_SIZE - 10, CANVAS_WIDTH * 0.2, 10);
                ctx.fillRect(CANVAS_WIDTH - 10, TILE_SIZE - 10, CANVAS_WIDTH * 0.8, 10);

                // Draw Cars (The moving elements)
                this.details.cars.forEach((car, i) => {
                    const x = car.x;
                    const yPos = Math.floor(y / TILE_SIZE); // Adjust Y slightly within the tile
                    ctx.fillStyle = `hsl(${i * 30 + 180}, 70%, 50%)`; // Varied color
                    ctx.fillRect(x, -TILE_SIZE + 5, car.w, TILE_SIZE - 10);
                });

                break;

            case 'River':
                // River: Blue water surface
                const waterGrad = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, CANVAS_WIDTH, 0);
                waterGrad.addColorStop(0, '#2980b9'); // Deep blue
                waterGrad.addColorStop(1, '#3498db'); // Sky blue
                ctx.fillStyle = waterGrad;
                ctx.shadowBlur = 15;
                ctx.fillRect(0, 0, CANVAS_WIDTH, TILE_SIZE);

                // Draw Logs/Rafts (Obstacle or safe path)
                if (this.details.logs) {
                    this.details.logs.forEach((log, i) => {
                        ctx.fillStyle = '#8b4513'; // Wood color
                        ctx.fillRect(log.x, -TILE_SIZE + 20, log.w, 30);
                        // Add simple shadow to lift it visually
                        ctx.shadowOffsetY(5);
                    });
                }
                break;

            case 'Railroad':
                // Railroad: Grey tracks on ballast
                const trackY = TILE_SIZE / 2 + 10; // Position slightly down
                const railColor = '#444';
                const ballastColor = '#7b7b7b';

                ctx.fillStyle = ballastColor;
                ctx.fillRect(0, TILE_SIZE - 20, CANVAS_WIDTH, 20);

                // Draw two tracks
                ctx.strokeStyle = railColor;
                ctx.lineWidth = 15;
                ctx.shadowBlur = 10;
                ctx.shadowColor = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3)';

                const startX = CANVAS_WIDTH / 2 - 30;
                const endX = CANVAS_WIDTH / 2 + 30;

                // Track 1 (Offset slightly)
                ctx.beginPath();
                ctx.moveTo(startX, trackY);
                ctx.lineTo(endX, trackY);
                ctx.stroke();

                // Draw Trains (moving element)
                this.details.trains.forEach((train, i) => {
                    const x = train.x;
                    ctx.fillStyle = `hsl(${i * 50 + 240}, 80%, 60%)`; // Varied bright color
                    // Train body
                    ctx.fillRect(x, -TILE_SIZE/2, train.w, TILE_SIZE - 10);

                    // Draw windows detail (for visual appeal)
                    ctx.fillStyle = '#ccc';
                    ctx.fillRect(x + 5, -TILE_SIZE/2 + 10, 10, 10);
                });

                break;

            case 'Coin':
                // Just a coin on a safe patch of grass
                const coinX = this.details.x;
                const coinY = TILE_SIZE * 0.8;
                ctx.fillStyle = '#ffcc00';
                ctx.strokeStyle = '#ffa500';
                ctx.lineWidth = 2;
                // Simple representation of a stacked voxel coin
                ctx.beginPath();
                ctx.ellipse(coinX, coinY, TILE_SIZE * 0.4, TILE_SIZE * 0.3, 0, 0, Math.PI * 2);
                ctx.fill();
                ctx.stroke();

                break;

        }
        ctx.restore();
    }
}


// --- GAME LOGIC AND MECHANICS ---

/** Generates the world for the next N rows of lanes */
function generateLane(yIndex) {
    const randomType = randInt(1, 100);
    let type;
    let details = {};

    if (randomType <= 35) {
        type = 'Grass';
    } else if (randomType <= 65) {
        type = 'Road';
        details.cars = [];
        // Generate 3 to 5 cars randomly spaced across the lane width
        for (let i = 0; i < randInt(3, 5); i++) {
            const xStart = randInt(0, CANVAS_WIDTH - TILE_SIZE * 0.2);
            details.cars.push({
                x: xStart,
                w: randInt(20, 40),
                speed: randInt(1, 3) + gameState.gameSpeedMultiplier * 0.5 // Difficulty ramp
            });
        }
    } else if (randomType <= 80) {
        type = 'River';
        details.logs = [];
         // Generate 2 to 4 logs/rafts
        for (let i = 0; i < randInt(2, 4); i++) {
            const xStart = randInt(0, CANVAS_WIDTH - TILE_SIZE * 0.3);
            details.logs.push({
                x: xStart,
                w: randInt(50, 100),
            });
        }
    } else if (randomType <= 90) {
        type = 'Railroad';
        details.trains = [];
         // Trains appear every few generations
        if (Math.random() > 0.3) {
            details.trains.push({
                x: randInt(50, CANVAS_WIDTH - 50),
                w: randInt(100, 200),
                speed: 8 // Always fast
            });
        } else {
             type = 'Grass'; // Fallback if no train is generated
             details.trains = [];
        }
    } else {
        // Coin chance (rare)
        if (Math.random() < 0.15) {
            type = 'Coin';
            details.x = randInt(20, CANVAS_WIDTH - 20);
        } else {
            type = 'Grass'; // Default fallback
        }
    }

    return new Lane(yIndex, type, details);
}


/** Initializes the world generation */
function initializeWorld() {
    lanes = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < LANE_GENERATION_COUNT; i++) {
        // Start generating from a random horizontal offset to make it dynamic
        const newLane = generateLane(i);
        lanes.push(newLane);
    }
}

/** Updates all moving elements and generates the next rows */
function updateWorld(deltaTime) {
    movers.time += deltaTime * 0.05; // Slow down train/car clock relative to game loop

    // Difficulty Ramp: Increase speed gradually (max increase after some time)
    gameState.difficultyTimer = Math.min(1, gameState.difficultyTimer + deltaTime / 3000);
    gameState.gameSpeedMultiplier = 1 + gameState.difficultyTimer * 1.5;


    // --- 1. Update Cars/Trains (Movers update) ---
    let newRoadDetails = {};
    let newRailDetails = {};

    for (const lane of lanes) {
        if (lane.type === 'Road') {
            newRoadDetails[lane.yIndex] = { details: [...lane.details.cars] };
            // Move cars left or right based on design (simplified to just move x-position towards the edge)
            for (let i = 0; i < lane.details.cars.length; i++) {
                const car = lane.details.cars[i];
                car.x += (car.speed * gameState.gameSpeedMultiplier) * (deltaTime / 16.6); // Scale movement
                if (car.x > CANVAS_WIDTH + 50) car.x = -50; // Wrap around or despaawn (wrapping is better for endless runner feel)
            }
        } else if (lane.type === 'Railroad') {
            newRailDetails[lane.yIndex] = { details: [...lane.details.trains] };
             for (let i = 0; i < lane.details.trains.length; i++) {
                const train = lane.details.trains[i];
                // Trains move from one side to the other repeatedly
                train.x += Math.sin(movers.time / 5) * (gameState.gameSpeedMultiplier * 3);
            }
        } else {
            newRoadDetails[lane.yIndex] = null;
            newRailDetails[lane.yIndex] = null;
        }
    }

    // Apply updated details back to the lanes array
    lanes.forEach(lane => {
        if (lane.type === 'Road') lane.details.cars = newRoadDetails[lane.yIndex]?.details || [];
        if (lane.type === 'Railroad') lane.details.trains = newRailDetails[lane.yIndex]?.details || [];
    });


    // --- 2. Process Hops and Scoring/Collision Check (Done in the input handler for simplicity) ---

    // --- 3. Management: Despawning Old Lanes & Generating New Ones ---
    const playerYGrid = Math.floor((player.y + TILE_SIZE / 2) / TILE_SIZE); // Normalized grid index where player currently is
    const currentLaneIndex = lanes.findIndex(l => l.yIndex === playerYGrid);

    // Clean up the front (Top/Lowest Y indices)
    if (lanes[0] && Math.abs(lanes[0].yIndex - playerYGrid) > LANE_GENERATION_COUNT + 5) {
        console.log("Despawning old lanes.");
        lanes.shift(); // Remove the top/oldest lane data
    }

    // Generate new rows ahead of the player (Target index = current highest Y grid index - N)
    if (lanes[lanes.length - 1] && Math.abs(lanes[lanes.length - 1].yIndex - (playerYGrid - LANE_GENERATION_COUNT)) > 5) {
        const newLevel = generateLane(Math.min(CANVAS_HEIGHT / TILE_SIZE, lanes[lanes.length - 1].yIndex - LANE_GENERATION_COUNT));
        // Add the new lane to the front (lowest Y index in our array representation)
        lanes.unshift(newLevel);
    }

    // --- 4. Coin Update (Simple particle generation) ---
    if (Math.random() < 0.1 && lanes[0].type === 'Coin') {
         particles.coinTrail.push({
            x: Math.random() * CANVAS_WIDTH,
            y: TILE_SIZE * (lanes[0].yIndex + 2), // Slightly below the coin spot
            vx: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 2,
            vy: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 2,
            life: 60
        });
    }

     // Update particles trail
     particles.coinTrail = particles.coinTrail.filter(p => p.life > 0);
     for (let i = 0; i < particles.coinTrail.length; i++) {
         particles.coinTrail[i].x += particles.coinTrail[i].vx;
         particles.coinTrail[i].y += particles.coinTrail[i].vy;
         particles.coinTrail[i].life--;
     }

}


// --- INPUT HANDLING ---

/** Executes a hop attempt given the direction and target lane index */
function tryHop(targetYIndex, targetX) {
    if (!gameRunning || player.isJumping) return false; // Cannot hop if currently airborne
    
    const currentLane = getLaneAtGridPosition(player.currentTileY);

    // Basic check: Is the target area occupied? (e.g., railway active, car right on top)
    if (!isValidTargetPosition(targetX)) {
        return false; // Cannot move there immediately
    }

    // Check collision at destination *before* moving
    const targetLane = getLaneAtGridPosition(targetYIndex);
    if (targetLane && checkCollision(player.size / TILE_SIZE, player.size / TILE_SIZE, targetX, 0)) {
        console.log("Blocked by obstacle!");
        return false;
    }

    // Successful hop initiation
    player.x = targetX;
    player.currentTileY = targetYIndex;
    player.y += player.speed * 2; // Quick visual movement up/down (CSS scaling for squash/stretch handled by draw)
    player.isJumping = true;
    setTimeout(() => {
        player.isJumping = false;
        // After the hop animation finishes, we must update the lane position data
        updatePlayerLaneData(); 
    }, 300);

    return true;
}


/** Determines which lane object is closest to a given grid Y coordinate */
function getLaneAtGridPosition(yIndex) {
    // Since lanes are sorted by yIndex (lowest index = top screen), we search based on the required Y position.
    const targetY = Math.floor((canvas.height - player.size / TILE_SIZE * 0.8) / TILE_SIZE);

    // Find the lane whose grid index matches the current or nearest desired grid position
    return lanes.find(l => l.yIndex === yIndex) || null;
}


/** Checks if a target X coordinate is clear on the current road/tile */
function isValidTargetPosition(targetX) {
     // Crude check: Ensure we aren't targeting directly inside a known hazard zone (e.g., railroad center, car path)
    if (getLaneAtGridPosition(player.currentTileY)) {
        const lane = getLaneAtGridPosition(player.currentTileY);

        if (lane.type === 'Road') {
            for (const car of lane.details.cars) {
                // If target is within the horizontal bounds of a moving vehicle, it's blocked
                if (targetX >= car.x && targetX <= car.x + car.w) return false;
            }
        }
        if (lane.type === 'Railroad') {
            const train = lane.details.trains[0];
             if (targetX >= train.x - 15 && targetX <= train.x + train.w + 15) return false;
        }
    }
    return true;
}


/** Collision Check: Checks for collision at player's current physical position */
function checkCollision(playerW, playerH, nextX, nextY) {
    const targetLane = getLaneAtGridPosition(nextY);

    if (!targetLane) return false; // No lane defined here

    switch (targetLane.type) {
        case 'Road':
            // Check against all moving cars
            for (const car of targetLane.details.cars) {
                if (isColliding(nextX, nextY, playerW * TILE_SIZE, playerH * TILE_SIZE, 
                                car.x, -TILE_SIZE + 5, car.w, TILE_SIZE - 10)) {
                    return true; // Hit a car!
                }
            }
            break;

        case 'River':
            // Check if the player is in water AND not on a log/raft.
             const logs = targetLane.details.logs || [];
             let safeFromWater = false;
             for (const log of logs) {
                 if (nextX + playerW * TILE_SIZE >= log.x && nextX - 10 <= log.x && 
                     nextY + playerH * TILE_SIZE >= 0 && nextY - 10 <= log.y + TILE_SIZE ) {
                        safeFromWater = true;
                        break;
                 }
             }
             if (!safeFromWater) return true; // Drowned! (Treating water contact as lethal if not supported)
            break;

        case 'Railroad':
            // Check against trains passing through the intersection point.
            const train = targetLane.details.trains[0];
            if (isColliding(nextX, nextY, playerW * TILE_SIZE, playerH * TILE_SIZE, 
                            train.x - 15, -TILE_SIZE/2, train.w + 30, TILE_SIZE)) { // Check collision box slightly bigger than the object
                return true; // Hit train!
            }
            break;

        case 'Coin':
             // Safe to land on a coin spot (we'll handle pickup later)
             return false;
    }

    return false;
}


/** Updates player state after successful hop */
function updatePlayerLaneData() {
    const targetLane = getLaneAtGridPosition(player.currentTileY);
    if (targetLane) {
        // Check for collision upon landing (This is the crucial death moment)
        if (checkCollision(player.size / TILE_SIZE, player.size / TILE_SIZE, player.x / TILE_SIZE, 0)) {
            gameOver("Collision detected!");
            return;
        }

        // Check for hazards on landing
        if (targetLane.type === 'River' && !targetLane.details.logs) {
            gameOver("You drowned.");
            return;
        }

        // Handle coin pickup immediately upon confirmation of landing in the tile center
        if (targetLane.type === 'Coin') {
             gameState.coins++;
             triggerSparkle(player.x, TILE_SIZE * (player.currentTileY + 1), 10); // Large sparkle
             // Temporarily despawn coin for visual feedback
             lanes[lanes.findIndex(l => l.type === 'Coin' && l.yIndex === player.currentTileY)].details.x = -99;
        }


    }

    // Score update: Every successful hop upward increments the score
    gameState.score += 1;
    updateUI();

    // Re-establish initial position if it was wildly off due to temporary movement adjustments
    player.y = player.currentTileY * TILE_SIZE + (TILE_SIZE / 2);
}


/** Primary Game Loop - Runs every frame */
function gameLoop(timestamp) {
    if (!gameRunning) return;

    const deltaTime = timestamp - lastTime;
    lastTime = timestamp;

    // --- Drawing & Rendering ---
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, CANVAS_WIDTH, CANVAS_HEIGHT);
    drawBackground();

    updateWorld(deltaTime); // Update positions and generate new lanes
    renderWorldAndPlayer();  // Draw all components

    // Handle Physics: Gravity (If we were building a complex falling physics)
    // For now, the "gravity" is handled entirely by player.currentTileY updates upon hopping/scrolling

    // Request next frame
    requestAnimationFrame(gameLoop);
}


/** Drawing Functions */

function drawBackground() {
    const gradient = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, 0, CANVAS_HEIGHT);
    gradient.addColorStop(0, '#ff6f91'); // Coral (Dawn start)
    gradient.addColorStop(0.5, '#c3b1e4'); // Lavender
    gradient.addColorStop(1, '#4d5c80');  // Deep blue (Twilight/Night)

    ctx.fillStyle = gradient;
    ctx.fillRect(0, 0, CANVAS_WIDTH, CANVAS_HEIGHT);

    // Draw subtle parallax clouds (simple white rects)
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.3)';
     for(let i=0; i < 10; i++){
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.ellipse((i*100 + Math.random()*50), Math.random()*150 + 50, 100, 20, 0, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fill();
    }

    // Draw ground level line (separating voxels from sky)
    ctx.fillStyle = '#4cbb17'; // Bright green base
    ctx.fillRect(0, CANVAS_HEIGHT - TILE_SIZE * 0.5, CANVAS_WIDTH, TILE_SIZE * 2);
}

function renderWorldAndPlayer() {
    // Use a virtual camera offset based on player's vertical progress
    const scrollYOffset = (player.currentTileY * TILE_SIZE) * 0.8; // Player moves up relative to the screen origin

    ctx.save();
    ctx.translate(0, -scrollYOffset); // Everything appears to move down the canvas as player hops/scrolls up

    // Render lanes (World background)
    for (const lane of lanes) {
        lane.draw(Math.floor((player.currentTileY + Math.abs(Math.pow(lane.yIndex - player.currentTileY), 2)) / 3)); // Simple y calculation for depth variation
    }

    // Render Player character (must be drawn last to appear on top)
    drawPlayer();

    ctx.restore();

    // Draw particles over everything
    particles.coinTrail.forEach(p => {
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255, 204, 0, 0.8)';
        ctx.globalAlpha = p.life / 60;
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(p.x, p.y, 3 + (p.life / 10), 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fill();
    });
     // Death Burst particles are only visible right at death
}

function drawPlayer() {
    const p = player;
    const sizePixels = p.size * TILE_SIZE / 100; // Scale down slightly for visual appeal

    ctx.save();
    // Apply squash/stretch effect based on `isJumping` state
    let scaleY = p.isJumping ? 1.2 : 1;
    let scaleX = p.isJumping ? 0.95 : 1;
    
    ctx.translate(p.x, p.y);
    ctx.scale(scaleX, scaleY);

    // Draw the Player Voxel block (Simple geometric shape)
    ctx.fillStyle = '#ff6f91'; // Primary vibrant color
    ctx.strokeStyle = '#cc5280';
    ctx.lineWidth = 3;
    ctx.fillRect(-sizePixels / 2, -sizePixels / 2, sizePixels, sizePixels);
    ctx.strokeRect(-sizePixels / 2, -sizePixels / 2, sizePixels, sizePixels);

    // Add an eye detail or internal glow for "premium" feel
     ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
     ctx.fillRect(sizePixels/8, -sizePixels/3, sizePixels/5, sizePixels/4);


    ctx.restore();
}


/** Particle Emitter */
function triggerSparkle(x, y, count) {
    for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
        particles.coinTrail.push({
            x: x + Math.random() * 20 - 10,
            y: y + Math.random() * 20 - 10,
            vx: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 8,
            vy: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 8,
            life: 90 // Longer life for a 'sparkle' effect
        });
    }
}


// --- GAME FLOW CONTROL ---

/** Initializes the score display and UI */
function updateUI() {
    document.getElementById('scoreDisplay').textContent = `Score: ${gameState.score}`;
    document.getElementById('coinCounter').innerHTML = `💰: ${gameState.coins}`;
}

/** Sets up the game environment for a fresh run */
function setupGame() {
    // Reset player state
    player.x = CANVAS_WIDTH / 2;
    player.y = canvas.height - (TILE_SIZE * 3);
    player.currentTileY = Math.floor((canvas.height - (TILE_SIZE * 3) + TILE_SIZE/2)/TILE_SIZE);

    gameState.score = 0;
    gameState.coins = 0;
    gameState.difficultyTimer = 0;
    movers.time = 0;
    particles.coinTrail = [];
}

/** Starts the game from the title screen */
function startGame() {
    document.getElementById('startScreen').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('gameOverScreen').style.display = 'none';
    setupGame();
    gameRunning = true;
    initializeWorld();
    lastTime = performance.now();
    requestAnimationFrame(gameLoop);
}

/** Handles death state */
function gameOver(reason) {
    if (!gameRunning) return; // Prevent double calls

    gameRunning = false;
    console.log("Game Over:", reason);

    // Trigger Death Particles (Screen Shake Start)
    for (let i = 0; i < 50; i++) {
        particles.deathBurst.push({
            x: player.x + Math.random() * 20 - 10,
            y: player.y + Math.random() * 20 - 10,
            vx: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 10,
            vy: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 10,
            life: 60,
        });
    }

    // Show Game Over Screen
    document.getElementById('finalScore').textContent = `Your Score: ${gameState.score}`;
    const bestScoreElement = document.getElementById('bestScoreDisplay');
    bestScoreElement.textContent = `Best Score: ${gameState.bestScore}`;
    document.getElementById('gameOverScreen').style.display = 'flex';

    // Gentle screen shake effect applied via CSS/JS logic in the final implementation structure, 
    // but here we simply stop game movement and display UI.
}


/** Resets the game for a new run */
function resetGame() {
    setupGame();
    initializeWorld(); // Re-generate map data
    document.getElementById('gameOverScreen').style.display = 'none';
    gameRunning = true;
    lastTime = performance.now();
    requestAnimationFrame(gameLoop);
}


// --- INPUT LISTENERS (Keyboard and Touch Simulation) ---

function handleInput() {
    let targetY = player.currentTileY;
    let nextX = player.x;
    let nextY = player.currentTileY; 

    // Determine intended movement based on the last known input or simple state machine:
    if (window.lastMove === 'UP') {
        nextY++; // Moving higher on the grid map (lower Y index)
    } else if (window.lastMove === 'DOWN') {
        nextY--; // Moving lower on the grid map (higher Y index)
    } else if (window.lastMove === 'LEFT') {
        nextX -= player.speed;
    } else if (window.lastMove === 'RIGHT') {
        nextX += player.speed;
    } else {
         // Default to trying an UP move if no directional input is received in a row
         nextY++; 
    }


    const hopSuccessful = tryHop(Math.max(0, nextY), Math.min(CANVAS_WIDTH - player.size * TILE_SIZE/100, nextX));

    if (hopSuccessful) {
        // If hop succeeds, update the move state for sequential hopping logic 
        window.lastMove = 'UP'; // Default successful movement to UP trajectory
    } else if (Math.key === 'ArrowLeft' || Math.key === 'a') {
        window.lastMove = 'LEFT';
    } else if (Math.key === 'ArrowRight' || Math.key === 'd') {
        window.lastMove = 'RIGHT';
    } else if (Math.key === 'ArrowUp' || Math.key === 'w') {
        window.lastMove = 'UP';
    } else if (Math.key === 'ArrowDown' || Math.key === 's') {
         window.lastMove = 'DOWN';
    }

}

// Global Input Handler (for both desktop and simulating touch)
document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
    if (!gameRunning && e.code === 'Space') {
        startGame();
    } else if (gameRunning) {
        e.preventDefault();
        handleInput();
    }
});

// Simple click/tap handler on the container to simulate WASD input and improve mobile usability
document.getElementById('gameContainer').addEventListener('click', () => {
    if (!gameRunning && !['titleScreen', 'gameOverScreen'].includes(document.getElementById('startScreen').style.display)) {
         // If game is not running, clicking the container does nothing unless the button is pressed.
        return; 
    }
    
    // Simple tap input model: Taps trigger an UP movement attempt (like a basic 'crossy' mechanic)
    if (gameRunning) {
        window.lastMove = 'UP'; // Treat click as upward hop attempt
        handleInput();
    }
});


// --- INITIALIZATION ON LOAD ---

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    updateUI(); 
});

</script>
</body>
</html>

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">

  html, body {
    width: 100%; height: 100%;

  #wrap {

</style>

<main id="wrap">
  <canvas id="game" aria-label="Voxel Hop arcade game"></canvas>
</main>
<script>
(function() {
'use strict';

const canvas = document.getElementById('game');
const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');

const VW = 540, VH = 960;
const GRID_W = 9;
const TW = 52, TH = 26, TD = 18;
const HALF_W = GRID_W >> 1;

const STATE = { TITLE: 'title', PLAYING: 'playing', GAMEOVER: 'gameover' };

const LANE = { GRASS: 0, ROAD: 1, RIVER: 2, RAIL: 3 };

const COLORS = {
  grassTop: '#6ecf68', grassLeft: '#4da84a', grassRight: '#5dbd56',
  roadTop: '#5a5a62', roadLeft: '#42424a', roadRight: '#4e4e56',
  waterTop: '#4ab8e0', waterLeft: '#2e8eb8', waterRight: '#3aa8d4',
  railTop: '#8a8078', railLeft: '#6a625c', railRight: '#787068',
  railMetal: '#c8c0b8', railWood: '#6a5040',
  playerTop: '#ff6b8a', playerLeft: '#d94a68', playerRight: '#f05a78',
  playerEye: '#2a1830',
  coinGold: '#ffd84a', coinShine: '#fff6b0',
  carColors: ['#ff5a4a','#4a9eff','#ffca3a','#9b5cff','#3ddc84'],
  truckColor: '#e8e0d0', logTop: '#a07040', logLeft: '#7a5530', logRight: '#906038',
  trainBody: '#d04040', trainDark: '#902828', cloud: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.55)'
};

let state = STATE.TITLE;
let score = 0, coins = 0, bestScore = 0;
let lanes = new Map();
let particles = [];
let screenShake = 0, freezeFrames = 0;
let cameraZ = 0, cameraTargetZ = 0;
let highestZ = 0;
let difficulty = 0;
let time = 0;
let titleBob = 0;
let logoPulse = 0;
let transitionAlpha = 0;
let dpr = 1;

try { bestScore = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('voxelHopBest') || '0', 10) || 0; } catch(e) {}

const player = {
  gx: 0, gz: 0,
  fromX: 0, fromZ: 0, toX: 0, toZ: 0,
  hopT: 1, hopDur: 0.18,
  squash: 1, alive: true,
  onLog: null,
  facing: 0
};

const keys = {};
let touchStart = null;
let pendingDir = null;

function seededRand(seed) {
  let s = seed | 0;
  return function() {
    s = (s + 0x6D2B79F5) | 0;
    let t = Math.imul(s ^ (s >>> 15), 1 | s);
    t = (t + Math.imul(t ^ (t >>> 7), 61 | t)) ^ t;
    return ((t ^ (t >>> 14)) >>> 0) / 4294967296;
  };
}

function laneSeed(z) { return (z * 7919 + 104729) | 0; }

function isoPos(gx, gz) {
  const cx = VW * 0.5;
  const cy = VH * 0.62;
  const cam = cameraZ;
  const sx = cx + (gx - gz + cam) * TW * 0.5;
  const sy = cy + (gx + gz - cam) * TH * 0.5;
  return { x: sx, y: sy };
}

function drawVoxelFace(sx, sy, w, h, d, top, left, right) {
  const hw = w * 0.5, hh = h * 0.5;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(sx, sy - hh);
  ctx.lineTo(sx + hw, sy);
  ctx.lineTo(sx, sy + hh);
  ctx.lineTo(sx - hw, sy);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.fillStyle = top;
  ctx.fill();

  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(sx, sy + hh);
  ctx.lineTo(sx + hw, sy);
  ctx.lineTo(sx + hw, sy + d);
  ctx.lineTo(sx, sy + hh + d);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.fillStyle = right;
  ctx.fill();

  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(sx, sy + hh);
  ctx.lineTo(sx - hw, sy);
  ctx.lineTo(sx - hw, sy + d);
  ctx.lineTo(sx, sy + hh + d);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.fillStyle = left;
  ctx.fill();
}

function drawGrassTile(sx, sy, variant) {
  const g = variant * 0.04;
  drawVoxelFace(sx, sy, TW, TH, TD,
    shade(COLORS.grassTop, g), shade(COLORS.grassLeft, g), shade(COLORS.grassRight, g));
  if (variant % 3 === 0) {
    ctx.fillStyle = '#3d9a3a';
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.arc(sx - 6, sy - 4, 2, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    ctx.arc(sx + 5, sy + 2, 1.5, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    ctx.fill();
  }
}

function drawRoadTile(sx, sy) {
  drawVoxelFace(sx, sy, TW, TH, TD - 4, COLORS.roadTop, COLORS.roadLeft, COLORS.roadRight);
  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,220,80,0.35)';
  ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;
  ctx.setLineDash([6, 8]);
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(sx - TW * 0.35, sy);
  ctx.lineTo(sx + TW * 0.35, sy);
  ctx.stroke();
  ctx.setLineDash([]);
}

function drawWaterTile(sx, sy, t) {
  drawVoxelFace(sx, sy, TW, TH, TD - 8, COLORS.waterTop, COLORS.waterLeft, COLORS.waterRight);
  const wave = Math.sin(t * 3 + sx * 0.05) * 2;
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(sx + wave, sy - 2, 10, 3, 0, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  ctx.fill();
}

function drawRailTile(sx, sy) {
  drawVoxelFace(sx, sy, TW, TH, TD - 6, COLORS.railTop, COLORS.railLeft, COLORS.railRight);
  const y = sy + 2;
  ctx.fillStyle = COLORS.railWood;
  ctx.fillRect(sx - TW * 0.4, y - 1, TW * 0.8, 3);
  ctx.strokeStyle = COLORS.railMetal;
  ctx.lineWidth = 2;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(sx - TW * 0.38, y - 3);
  ctx.lineTo(sx + TW * 0.38, y - 3);
  ctx.moveTo(sx - TW * 0.38, y + 4);
  ctx.lineTo(sx + TW * 0.38, y + 4);
  ctx.stroke();
}

function shade(hex, amt) {
  const n = parseInt(hex.slice(1), 16);
  let r = (n >> 16) & 255, g = (n >> 8) & 255, b = n & 255;
  r = Math.min(255, Math.max(0, r + amt * 255));
  g = Math.min(255, Math.max(0, g + amt * 255));
  b = Math.min(255, Math.max(0, b + amt * 255));
  return `rgb(${r|0},${g|0},${b|0})`;
}

function createLane(z) {
  const rand = seededRand(laneSeed(z));
  const d = difficulty + z * 0.02;
  let type;
  const r = rand();
  if (z <= 2) type = LANE.GRASS;
  else if (r < 0.32 - d * 0.02) type = LANE.GRASS;
  else if (r < 0.58) type = LANE.ROAD;
  else if (r < 0.82) type = LANE.RIVER;
  else type = LANE.RAIL;

  const lane = { z, type, vehicles: [], logs: [], train: null, coins: [], rand };

  if (type === LANE.ROAD) {
    const count = 1 + (rand() * 2 | 0);
    const dir = rand() > 0.5 ? 1 : -1;
    const baseSpeed = (2.2 + rand() * 1.5 + d * 0.4) * dir;
    for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
      const isTruck = rand() > 0.65;
      const len = isTruck ? 2.2 : 1.4;
      lane.vehicles.push({
        x: (rand() - 0.5) * (GRID_W + 4),
        speed: baseSpeed * (0.8 + rand() * 0.4),
        len, isTruck,
        color: isTruck ? COLORS.truckColor : COLORS.carColors[(rand() * 5) | 0],
        wheelPhase: rand() * 6.28
      });
    }
  }

  if (type === LANE.RIVER) {
    const count = 2 + (rand() * 2 | 0);
    const dir = rand() > 0.5 ? 1 : -1;
    for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
      lane.logs.push({
        x: (rand() - 0.5) * (GRID_W + 6),
        speed: (1.6 + rand() * 0.8 + d * 0.15) * dir,
        len: 2 + (rand() * 1.5 | 0)
      });
    }
  }

  if (type === LANE.RAIL) {
    lane.train = {
      active: false,
      x: -GRID_W - 6,
      timer: 2 + rand() * 4,
      speed: 9 + d * 0.8,
      cars: 4 + (rand() * 3 | 0)
    };
  }

  if (type === LANE.GRASS || (type === LANE.ROAD && rand() > 0.5)) {
    const numCoins = rand() > 0.55 ? 1 : 0;
    for (let i = 0; i < numCoins; i++) {
      const cx = ((rand() * (GRID_W - 2)) | 0) - HALF_W + 1;
      lane.coins.push({ x: cx, taken: false });
    }
  }

  return lane;
}

function ensureLanes() {
  const minZ = Math.floor(player.gz) - 8;
  const maxZ = Math.floor(player.gz) + 22;
  for (let z = minZ; z <= maxZ; z++) {
    if (!lanes.has(z)) lanes.set(z, createLane(z));
  }
  for (const z of [...lanes.keys()]) {
    if (z < minZ - 2 || z > maxZ + 2) lanes.delete(z);
  }
}

function getLane(z) {
  if (!lanes.has(z)) lanes.set(z, createLane(z));
  return lanes.get(z);
}

function hopDir(dx, dz) {
  if (state !== STATE.PLAYING || !player.alive || player.hopT < 1) return;
  const nx = player.gx + dx, nz = player.gz + dz;
  if (nx < -HALF_W || nx > HALF_W - 1) return;
  if (nz < 0) return;
  player.fromX = player.gx; player.fromZ = player.gz;
  player.toX = nx; player.toZ = nz;
  player.gx = nx; player.gz = nz;
  player.hopT = 0;
  player.squash = 0.65;
  if (dz > 0) player.facing = 2;
  else if (dz < 0) player.facing = 0;
  else if (dx > 0) player.facing = 3;
  else if (dx < 0) player.facing = 1;
}

function playerWorldPos() {
  const t = easeOutBack(player.hopT);
  const gx = player.fromX + (player.toX - player.fromX) * t;
  const gz = player.fromZ + (player.toZ - player.fromZ) * t;
  const p = isoPos(gx, gz);
  const hopY = Math.sin(player.hopT * Math.PI) * 22;
  return { gx, gz, x: p.x, y: p.y - hopY, t };
}

function easeOutBack(t) {
  const c1 = 1.70158, c3 = c1 + 1;
  return 1 + c3 * Math.pow(t - 1, 3) + c1 * Math.pow(t - 1, 2);
}

function spawnParticles(x, y, color, count, speed, life) {
  for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
    const a = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;
    const sp = speed * (0.5 + Math.random());
    particles.push({
      x, y, vx: Math.cos(a) * sp, vy: Math.sin(a) * sp - 2,
      life: life * (0.6 + Math.random() * 0.4), maxLife: life,
      color, size: 2 + Math.random() * 4
    });
  }
}

function spawnCoinSparkle(x, y) {
  for (let i = 0; i < 12; i++) {
    const a = (i / 12) * Math.PI * 2;
    particles.push({
      x, y, vx: Math.cos(a) * 3, vy: Math.sin(a) * 3 - 1,
      life: 0.5, maxLife: 0.5, color: COLORS.coinGold, size: 3
    });
  }
}

function killPlayer() {
  if (!player.alive) return;
  player.alive = false;
  const p = playerWorldPos();
  spawnParticles(p.x, p.y - 10, COLORS.playerTop, 28, 6, 0.8);
  spawnParticles(p.x, p.y - 10, '#fff', 12, 4, 0.6);
  screenShake = 14;
  freezeFrames = 18;
  setTimeout(() => {
    state = STATE.GAMEOVER;
    transitionAlpha = 0;
    if (score > bestScore) {
      bestScore = score;
      try { localStorage.setItem('voxelHopBest', String(bestScore)); } catch(e) {}
    }
  }, 900);
}

function checkCollisions() {
  const wp = playerWorldPos();
  const lane = getLane(Math.round(wp.gz));
  const px = wp.gx;

  if (lane.type === LANE.ROAD) {
    for (const v of lane.vehicles) {
      if (Math.abs(px - v.x) < v.len * 0.55) killPlayer();
    }
  }

  if (lane.type === LANE.RIVER && player.hopT > 0.4) {
    let onLog = false;
    for (const log of lane.logs) {
      if (Math.abs(px - log.x) < log.len * 0.48) {
        onLog = true;
        const drift = log.speed * 0.016;
        player.gx += drift;
        player.fromX += drift;
        player.toX += drift;
        if (player.gx < -HALF_W - 0.5 || player.gx > HALF_W - 0.5) killPlayer();
        break;
      }
    }
    if (!onLog) killPlayer();
  }

  if (lane.type === LANE.RAIL && lane.train && lane.train.active) {
    const train = lane.train;
    const trainLen = train.cars * 1.8 + 2;
    if (Math.abs(px - train.x) < trainLen * 0.5) killPlayer();
  }

  for (const c of lane.coins) {
    if (!c.taken && Math.abs(px - c.x) < 0.45 && Math.abs(player.gz - lane.z) < 0.3) {
      c.taken = true;
      coins++;
      score += 5;
      const p = isoPos(c.x, lane.z);
      spawnCoinSparkle(p.x, p.y - 14);
    }
  }
}

function updateLaneEntities(dt) {
  difficulty = Math.min(3, score * 0.02 + player.gz * 0.008);
  for (const lane of lanes.values()) {
    if (lane.type === LANE.ROAD) {
      const wrap = GRID_W + 6;
      for (const v of lane.vehicles) {
        v.x += v.speed * dt;
        v.wheelPhase += Math.abs(v.speed) * dt * 4;
        if (v.x > wrap) v.x = -wrap;
        if (v.x < -wrap) v.x = wrap;
      }
    }
    if (lane.type === LANE.RIVER) {
      const wrap = GRID_W + 8;
      for (const log of lane.logs) {
        log.x += log.speed * dt;
        if (log.x > wrap) log.x = -wrap;
        if (log.x < -wrap) log.x = wrap;
      }
    }
    if (lane.type === LANE.RAIL && lane.train) {
      const tr = lane.train;
      tr.timer -= dt;
      if (!tr.active && tr.timer <= 0) {
        tr.active = true;
        tr.x = -GRID_W - 8;
        tr.warn = 0.6;
      }
      if (tr.active) {
        tr.x += tr.speed * dt;
        if (tr.x > GRID_W + 12) {
          tr.active = false;
          tr.timer = 3 + Math.random() * 5 - difficulty * 0.3;
        }
      }
      if (tr.warn > 0) tr.warn -= dt;
    }
  }
}

function update(dt) {
  time += dt;
  titleBob += dt;
  logoPulse += dt * 2;

  if (freezeFrames > 0) { freezeFrames--; return; }

  if (state === STATE.TITLE) {
    transitionAlpha = Math.min(1, transitionAlpha + dt * 2);
    return;
  }

  if (state === STATE.PLAYING && player.alive) {
    if (player.hopT < 1) {
      player.hopT = Math.min(1, player.hopT + dt / player.hopDur);
      player.squash = 0.65 + (player.hopT) * 0.35;
      if (player.hopT >= 1) player.squash = 1;
    }

    if (pendingDir) {
      hopDir(pendingDir.dx, pendingDir.dz);
      pendingDir = null;
    }

    const prevHigh = highestZ;
    if (player.gz > highestZ) highestZ = Math.floor(player.gz);
    if (highestZ > prevHigh) score += highestZ - prevHigh;

    cameraTargetZ = player.gz;
    cameraZ += (cameraTargetZ - cameraZ) * Math.min(1, dt * 6);

    ensureLanes();
    updateLaneEntities(dt);
    checkCollisions();
  }

  if (state === STATE.GAMEOVER) {
    transitionAlpha = Math.min(1, transitionAlpha + dt * 3);
  }

  for (let i = particles.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    const p = particles[i];
    p.life -= dt;
    p.x += p.vx;
    p.y += p.vy;
    p.vy += 12 * dt;
    if (p.life <= 0) particles.splice(i, 1);
  }

  if (screenShake > 0) screenShake *= 0.85;
}

function drawSky() {
  const g = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, 0, 0, VH);
  g.addColorStop(0, '#ff8a6a');
  g.addColorStop(0.35, '#c49ae8');
  g.addColorStop(0.7, '#6a7fd4');
  g.addColorStop(1, '#2a3a78');
  ctx.fillStyle = g;
  ctx.fillRect(0, 0, VW, VH);

  const clouds = [
    { x: 80, y: 120, s: 1.2, sp: 0.15 },
    { x: 320, y: 180, s: 0.9, sp: 0.1 },
    { x: 450, y: 90, s: 1.0, sp: 0.12 },
    { x: 200, y: 260, s: 0.7, sp: 0.08 }
  ];
  for (const c of clouds) {
    const ox = ((time * c.sp * 20) % (VW + 100)) - 50;
    drawCloud(c.x + ox * 0.3, c.y, c.s);
    drawCloud(c.x + ox, c.y + 30, c.s * 0.8);
  }
}

function drawCloud(x, y, scale) {
  ctx.fillStyle = COLORS.cloud;
  const r = 18 * scale;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.arc(x, y, r, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  ctx.arc(x + r * 0.9, y - r * 0.2, r * 0.75, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  ctx.arc(x + r * 1.7, y, r * 0.65, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  ctx.arc(x + r * 0.5, y + r * 0.3, r * 0.55, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  ctx.fill();
}

function drawVehicle(sx, sy, v) {
  const w = TW * v.len * 0.45;
  const h = TH * 0.7;
  const d = TD * 0.8;
  drawVoxelFace(sx, sy - 6, w, h, d, v.color, shade(v.color, -0.15), shade(v.color, -0.08));
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(180,220,255,0.7)';
  const fw = w * 0.22;
  ctx.fillRect(sx - fw * 0.3, sy - h * 0.35, fw, h * 0.35);
  ctx.fillStyle = '#333';
  const wp = v.wheelPhase;
  for (let i = -1; i <= 1; i += 2) {
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.arc(sx + i * w * 0.28, sy + h * 0.25, 4, wp, wp + Math.PI * 2);
    ctx.fill();
  }
  if (v.isTruck) {
    ctx.fillStyle = shade(v.color, -0.2);
    ctx.fillRect(sx - w * 0.1, sy - h * 0.5, w * 0.5, h * 0.3);
  }
}

function drawLog(sx, sy, log) {
  const w = TW * log.len * 0.42;
  drawVoxelFace(sx, sy - 4, w, TH * 0.55, TD * 0.5, COLORS.logTop, COLORS.logLeft, COLORS.logRight);
  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(60,40,20,0.4)';
  ctx.lineWidth = 1;
  for (let i = -1; i <= 1; i++) {
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(sx + i * w * 0.25, sy - 6);
    ctx.lineTo(sx + i * w * 0.25, sy + 6);
    ctx.stroke();
  }
}

function drawTrain(sx, sy, train) {
  const carW = TW * 0.85;
  for (let i = 0; i < train.cars; i++) {
    const ox = (i - train.cars * 0.5) * carW;
    const col = i === 0 ? COLORS.trainBody : shade(COLORS.trainBody, -0.05 * i);
    drawVoxelFace(sx + ox, sy - 8, carW, TH * 0.85, TD * 1.1, col, COLORS.trainDark, shade(col, -0.1));
    if (i === 0) {
      ctx.fillStyle = '#ffee88';
      ctx.fillRect(sx + ox + carW * 0.15, sy - TH * 0.5, 8, 6);
    }
  }
}

function drawCoin(sx, sy, bob) {
  const by = sy - 16 + Math.sin(bob) * 3;
  ctx.fillStyle = COLORS.coinGold;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(sx, by, 8, 10, 0, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  ctx.fill();
  ctx.fillStyle = COLORS.coinShine;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.ellipse(sx - 2, by - 3, 3, 4, -0.4, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  ctx.fill();
  ctx.fillStyle = '#c8a020';
  ctx.font = 'bold 9px sans-serif';
  ctx.textAlign = 'center';
  ctx.fillText('¢', sx, by + 3);
}

function drawPlayerChar(sx, sy, squash, isTitle) {
  const sc = squash;
  const w = TW * 0.38, h = TH * 0.75 * sc, d = TD * 0.9;
  const bounce = isTitle ? Math.sin(titleBob * 3) * 6 : 0;
  drawVoxelFace(sx, sy - 12 + bounce, w, h, d,
    COLORS.playerTop, COLORS.playerLeft, COLORS.playerRight);
  ctx.fillStyle = COLORS.playerEye;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.arc(sx - 4, sy - 18 + bounce, 2.5, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  ctx.arc(sx + 4, sy - 18 + bounce, 2.5, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  ctx.fill();
  ctx.fillStyle = '#fff';
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.arc(sx - 3, sy - 19 + bounce, 1, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  ctx.arc(sx + 5, sy - 19 + bounce, 1, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  ctx.fill();
}

function drawWorld() {
  const drawList = [];

  for (const lane of lanes.values()) {
    for (let gx = -HALF_W; gx < HALF_W; gx++) {
      const p = isoPos(gx, lane.z);
      drawList.push({ depth: gx + lane.z, type: 'tile', lane, gx, p });
    }
    for (const c of lane.coins) {
      if (!c.taken) {
        const p = isoPos(c.x, lane.z);
        drawList.push({ depth: c.x + lane.z + 0.1, type: 'coin', lane, c, p });
      }
    }
    if (lane.type === LANE.ROAD) {
      for (const v of lane.vehicles) {
        const p = isoPos(v.x, lane.z);
        drawList.push({ depth: v.x + lane.z + 0.2, type: 'vehicle', v, p });
      }
    }
    if (lane.type === LANE.RIVER) {
      for (const log of lane.logs) {
        const p = isoPos(log.x, lane.z);
        drawList.push({ depth: log.x + lane.z + 0.15, type: 'log', log, p });
      }
    }
    if (lane.type === LANE.RAIL && lane.train && lane.train.active) {
      const p = isoPos(lane.train.x, lane.z);
      drawList.push({ depth: lane.train.x + lane.z + 0.25, type: 'train', train: lane.train, p });
    }
  }

  const pp = playerWorldPos();
  if (state === STATE.PLAYING) {
    drawList.push({ depth: pp.gx + pp.gz + 0.3, type: 'player', p: pp });
  }

  drawList.sort((a, b) => a.depth - b.depth);

  for (const item of drawList) {
    if (item.type === 'tile') {
      const { lane, gx, p } = item;
      const variant = (lane.z + gx) & 7;
      if (lane.type === LANE.GRASS) drawGrassTile(p.x, p.y, variant);
      else if (lane.type === LANE.ROAD) drawRoadTile(p.x, p.y);
      else if (lane.type === LANE.RIVER) drawWaterTile(p.x, p.y, time + lane.z);
      else drawRailTile(p.x, p.y);
      if (lane.type === LANE.RAIL && lane.train && lane.train.warn > 0) {
        ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(255,80,60,${0.3 + Math.sin(time * 12) * 0.2})`;
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(p.x, p.y - 20, 6, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        ctx.fill();
      }
    } else if (item.type === 'coin') {
      drawCoin(item.p.x, item.p.y, time * 4 + item.c.x);
    } else if (item.type === 'vehicle') {
      drawVehicle(item.p.x, item.p.y, item.v);
    } else if (item.type === 'log') {
      drawLog(item.p.x, item.p.y, item.log);
    } else if (item.type === 'train') {
      drawTrain(item.p.x, item.p.y, item.train);
    } else if (item.type === 'player') {
      drawPlayerChar(item.p.x, item.p.y, player.squash, false);
    }
  }
}

function roundRect(x, y, w, h, r) {
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(x + r, y);
  ctx.arcTo(x + w, y, x + w, y + h, r);
  ctx.arcTo(x + w, y + h, x, y + h, r);
  ctx.arcTo(x, y + h, x, y, r);
  ctx.arcTo(x, y, x + w, y, r);
  ctx.closePath();
}

function drawUI() {
  if (state === STATE.PLAYING || state === STATE.GAMEOVER) {
    ctx.save();
    roundRect(VW * 0.5 - 52, 18, 104, 36, 18);
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(20,16,40,0.55)';
    ctx.fill();
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.2)';
    ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;
    ctx.stroke();
    ctx.fillStyle = '#fff';
    ctx.font = 'bold 20px -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, sans-serif';
    ctx.textAlign = 'center';
    ctx.fillText(String(score), VW * 0.5, 43);

    roundRect(18, 18, 88, 36, 18);
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(20,16,40,0.55)';
    ctx.fill();
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.2)';
    ctx.stroke();
    ctx.fillStyle = COLORS.coinGold;
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.arc(38, 36, 9, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    ctx.fill();
    ctx.fillStyle = '#c8a020';
    ctx.font = 'bold 8px sans-serif';
    ctx.fillText('¢', 38, 39);
    ctx.fillStyle = '#fff';
    ctx.font = 'bold 18px sans-serif';
    ctx.textAlign = 'left';
    ctx.fillText(String(coins), 54, 42);

    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.5)';
    ctx.font = '12px sans-serif';
    ctx.textAlign = 'right';
    ctx.fillText('BEST ' + bestScore, VW - 18, 42);
    ctx.restore();
  }
}

function drawTitle() {
  ctx.save();
  ctx.globalAlpha = transitionAlpha;

  const logoY = VH * 0.22 + Math.sin(logoPulse) * 4;
  ctx.textAlign = 'center';
  ctx.font = 'bold 52px -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, sans-serif';
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.25)';
  ctx.fillText('VOXEL', VW * 0.5 + 3, logoY + 3);
  ctx.fillText('HOP', VW * 0.5 + 3, logoY + 55);
  const lg = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, logoY - 30, 0, logoY + 70);
  lg.addColorStop(0, '#fff');
  lg.addColorStop(0.5, '#ffe0a0');
  lg.addColorStop(1, '#ff8a9a');
  ctx.fillStyle = lg;
  ctx.fillText('VOXEL', VW * 0.5, logoY);
  ctx.fillText('HOP', VW * 0.5, logoY + 52);

  const charP = isoPos(0, 2);
  drawPlayerChar(charP.x, charP.y + 40 + Math.sin(titleBob * 2) * 10, 1, true);

  const pulse = 0.6 + Math.sin(time * 3) * 0.4;
  ctx.globalAlpha = transitionAlpha * pulse;
  ctx.fillStyle = '#fff';
  ctx.font = '18px -apple-system, sans-serif';
  ctx.fillText('Press Space or Tap to Play', VW * 0.5, VH * 0.78);

  ctx.globalAlpha = transitionAlpha * 0.5;
  ctx.font = '13px sans-serif';
  ctx.fillText('Arrow keys / WASD / Swipe to move', VW * 0.5, VH * 0.84);
  ctx.restore();
}

function drawGameOver() {
  ctx.save();
  ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(10,8,24,${0.55 * transitionAlpha})`;
  ctx.fillRect(0, 0, VW, VH);

  const cx = VW * 0.5, cy = VH * 0.42;
  roundRect(cx - 140, cy - 90, 280, 200, 24);
  ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(30,24,50,${0.92 * transitionAlpha})`;
  ctx.fill();
  ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(255,255,255,${0.15 * transitionAlpha})`;
  ctx.lineWidth = 2;
  ctx.stroke();

  ctx.globalAlpha = transitionAlpha;
  ctx.textAlign = 'center';
  ctx.fillStyle = '#ff6b7a';
  ctx.font = 'bold 32px sans-serif';
  ctx.fillText('GAME OVER', cx, cy - 40);
  ctx.fillStyle = '#fff';
  ctx.font = '22px sans-serif';
  ctx.fillText('Score: ' + score, cx, cy + 5);
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.6)';
  ctx.font = '16px sans-serif';
  ctx.fillText('Best: ' + bestScore, cx, cy + 35);

  const btnPulse = 0.85 + Math.sin(time * 4) * 0.15;
  roundRect(cx - 90, cy + 58, 180, 44, 22);
  ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(255,107,138,${btnPulse})`;
  ctx.fill();
  ctx.fillStyle = '#fff';
  ctx.font = 'bold 18px sans-serif';
  ctx.fillText('Play Again', cx, cy + 86);
  ctx.restore();
}

function drawParticlesLayer() {
  for (const p of particles) {
    const a = p.life / p.maxLife;
    ctx.globalAlpha = a;
    ctx.fillStyle = p.color;
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.arc(p.x, p.y, p.size * a, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    ctx.fill();
  }
  ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
}

function render() {
  ctx.save();
  let sx = 0, sy = 0;
  if (screenShake > 0.5) {
    sx = (Math.random() - 0.5) * screenShake;
    sy = (Math.random() - 0.5) * screenShake;
  }
  ctx.translate(sx, sy);

  drawSky();

  if (state !== STATE.TITLE) drawWorld();

  drawParticlesLayer();
  drawUI();

  if (state === STATE.TITLE) drawTitle();
  if (state === STATE.GAMEOVER) drawGameOver();

  ctx.restore();
}

function resetGame() {
  score = 0; coins = 0;
  highestZ = 0; difficulty = 0;
  cameraZ = 0; cameraTargetZ = 0;
  lanes.clear();
  particles = [];
  screenShake = 0; freezeFrames = 0;
  player.gx = 0; player.gz = 0;
  player.fromX = 0; player.fromZ = 0;
  player.toX = 0; player.toZ = 0;
  player.hopT = 1; player.squash = 1;
  player.alive = true; player.facing = 2;
  for (let z = 0; z <= 18; z++) lanes.set(z, createLane(z));
  ensureLanes();
}

function startGame() {
  resetGame();
  state = STATE.PLAYING;
  transitionAlpha = 1;
}

function resize() {
  dpr = Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio || 1, 2);
  const aspect = VW / VH;
  let w = window.innerWidth, h = window.innerHeight;
  if (w / h > aspect) w = h * aspect;
  else h = w / aspect;
  canvas.style.width = w + 'px';
  canvas.style.height = h + 'px';
  canvas.width = VW * dpr;
  canvas.height = VH * dpr;
  ctx.setTransform(dpr, 0, 0, dpr, 0, 0);
}

function handleKey(e, down) {
  const k = e.key.toLowerCase();
  keys[k] = down;
  if (!down) return;

  if (state === STATE.TITLE && (k === ' ' || k === 'enter')) {
    e.preventDefault();
    startGame();
    return;
  }
  if (state === STATE.GAMEOVER && (k === ' ' || k === 'enter')) {
    e.preventDefault();
    startGame();
    return;
  }
  if (state !== STATE.PLAYING) return;

  if (k === 'arrowup' || k === 'w') hopDir(0, 1);
  else if (k === 'arrowdown' || k === 's') hopDir(0, -1);
  else if (k === 'arrowleft' || k === 'a') hopDir(-1, 0);
  else if (k === 'arrowright' || k === 'd') hopDir(1, 0);
}

window.addEventListener('keydown', e => handleKey(e, true));
window.addEventListener('keyup', e => { keys[e.key.toLowerCase()] = false; });

canvas.addEventListener('pointerdown', e => {
  const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
  touchStart = {
    x: e.clientX - rect.left,
    y: e.clientY - rect.top,
    time: performance.now(),
    sw: rect.width, sh: rect.height
  };
});

canvas.addEventListener('pointerup', e => {
  if (!touchStart) return;
  const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
  const ex = e.clientX - rect.left;
  const ey = e.clientY - rect.top;
  const dx = ex - touchStart.x;
  const dy = ey - touchStart.y;
  const dist = Math.hypot(dx, dy);
  const elapsed = performance.now() - touchStart.time;

  if (state === STATE.TITLE || state === STATE.GAMEOVER) {
    if (dist < 30 && elapsed < 400) {
      if (state === STATE.GAMEOVER) {
        const cx = touchStart.sw * 0.5, cy = touchStart.sh * 0.52;
        if (Math.abs(touchStart.x - cx) < 100 && Math.abs(touchStart.y - cy) < 80) startGame();
        else startGame();
      } else startGame();
    }
    touchStart = null;
    return;
  }

  if (dist < 18 && elapsed < 300) {
    const zx = touchStart.sw * 0.5, zy = touchStart.sh * 0.5;
    const tdx = touchStart.x - zx, tdy = touchStart.y - zy;
    if (Math.abs(tdx) > Math.abs(tdy)) pendingDir = { dx: tdx > 0 ? 1 : -1, dz: 0 };
    else pendingDir = { dx: 0, dz: tdy > 0 ? -1 : 1 };
  } else if (dist >= 18) {
    if (Math.abs(dx) > Math.abs(dy)) pendingDir = { dx: dx > 0 ? 1 : -1, dz: 0 };
    else pendingDir = { dx: 0, dz: dy < 0 ? 1 : -1 };
  }
  touchStart = null;
});

window.addEventListener('resize', resize);

let lastTime = performance.now();
function loop(now) {
  const dt = Math.min(0.05, (now - lastTime) / 1000);
  lastTime = now;
  update(dt);
  render();
  requestAnimationFrame(loop);
}

transitionAlpha = 0;
resize();
for (let z = 0; z <= 12; z++) lanes.set(z, createLane(z));
requestAnimationFrame(loop);

})();
</script>
</body>
</html>
```

<script>
const c=document.getElementById('c');
const ctx=c.getContext('2d');
const scoreEl=document.getElementById('scoreVal'), bestEl=document.getElementById('bestVal'), coinEl=document.getElementById('coinVal');
const goScore=document.getElementById('goScore'), goBest=document.getElementById('goBest');
const titleScreen=document.getElementById('title-screen'), gameoverScreen=document.getElementById('gameover-screen'), hud=document.getElementById('hud');

const COLS=13;
let W,H,DPR,TILE_W,TILE_H,centerX,centerY;
let cameraY=0, shake=0, shakeX=0, shakeY=0, time=0, lastTime=0;
let state='title';
let rows=[], particles=[], clouds=[];
let score=0, best=0, coins=0, startRow=2, maxRow=2;
let player, freezeTime=0;

function resize(){
  DPR=Math.min(window.devicePixelRatio||1,2);
  W=window.innerWidth*DPR; H=window.innerHeight*DPR;
  c.width=W; c.height=H;
  TILE_W=W*0.055; TILE_H=TILE_W*0.55;
  centerX=W/2; centerY=H*0.82;
}
function rand(a,b){ return a+Math.random()*(b-a); }
function randInt(a,b){ return Math.floor(rand(a,b+1)); }
function lerp(a,b,t){ return a+(b-a)*t; }
function shadeColor(col,p){
  const num=parseInt(col.replace('#',''),16);
  const amt=Math.round(2.55*p);
  let R=(num>>16)+amt,G=((num>>8)&0x00FF)+amt,B=(num&0x0000FF)+amt;
  R=R<0?0:R>255?255:R; G=G<0?0:G>255?255:G; B=B<0?0:B>255?255:B;
  return '#'+((1<<24)+(R<<16)+(G<<8)+B).toString(16).slice(1);
}

function iso(x,y,z=0){ return { x:(x-y)*TILE_W/2 + centerX + shakeX, y:(x+y)*TILE_H/2 + centerY + cameraY + shakeY - z*TILE_H*0.95 }; }
function drawBlock(x,y,z,w,l,h,topC){
  const s1=shadeColor(topC,-22), s2=shadeColor(topC,-40);
  const p000=iso(x,y,z), p100=iso(x+w,y,z), p010=iso(x,y+l,z), p110=iso(x+w,y+l,z);
  const p001=iso(x,y,z+h), p101=iso(x+w,y,z+h), p011=iso(x,y+l,z+h), p111=iso(x+w,y+l,z+h);
  ctx.fillStyle=s1; ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(p101.x,p101.y); ctx.lineTo(p100.x,p100.y); ctx.lineTo(p110.x,p110.y); ctx.lineTo(p111.x,p111.y); ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();
  ctx.fillStyle=s2; ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(p011.x,p011.y); ctx.lineTo(p010.x,p010.y); ctx.lineTo(p110.x,p110.y); ctx.lineTo(p111.x,p111.y); ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();
  ctx.fillStyle=topC; ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(p001.x,p001.y); ctx.lineTo(p101.x,p101.y); ctx.lineTo(p111.x,p111.y); ctx.lineTo(p011.x,p011.y); ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();
}
function drawLine(a,b, color, width){
  ctx.strokeStyle=color; ctx.lineWidth=width; ctx.lineCap='round';
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(a.x,a.y); ctx.lineTo(b.x,b.y); ctx.stroke();
}

function randomCarColor(){ return ['#ef5350','#42a5f5','#ffca28','#66bb6a','#ab47bc','#26c6da','#ffa726'][randInt(0,6)]; }
function randomFlowerColor(){ return ['#e91e63','#ffeb3b','#9c27b0','#00bcd4'][randInt(0,3)]; }

function drawSky(){
  const g=ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,0,H);
  g.addColorStop(0,'#0d1b3e'); g.addColorStop(0.45,'#6a4c93'); g.addColorStop(0.85,'#ff8a65'); g.addColorStop(1,'#ffcc80');
  ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,H);
}
function initClouds(){
  clouds=[];
  for(let i=0;i<8;i++) clouds.push({x:Math.random()*(W+400)-200, y:Math.random()*H*0.55, scale:0.4+Math.random()*1.3, speed:rand(4,18)});
}
function updateClouds(dt){
  clouds.forEach(cl=>{ cl.x-=cl.speed*dt*18; if(cl.x<-250) cl.x=W+250; });
}
function drawClouds(){
  clouds.forEach(cl=>{
    ctx.fillStyle='rgba(255,255,255,0.12)';
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.ellipse(cl.x,cl.y,70*cl.scale,28*cl.scale,0,0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.ellipse(cl.x+45*cl.scale,cl.y+12*cl.scale,55*cl.scale,24*cl.scale,0,0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.ellipse(cl.x-45*cl.scale,cl.y+6*cl.scale,50*cl.scale,22*cl.scale,0,0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fill();
  });
}

function chooseType(prev){
  const r=Math.random();
  if(prev==='water') return r<0.5?'grass':'road';
  if(prev==='rail') return r<0.55?'grass':'road';
  if(r<0.42) return 'grass';
  if(r<0.68) return 'road';
  if(r<0.87) return 'water';
  return 'rail';
}
function populateRoad(lane){
  const n=randInt(1,Math.min(4,2+Math.floor(score/120)));
  for(let i=0;i<n;i++){
    const isTruck=Math.random()<0.25;
    const length=isTruck?1.8:0.95;
    const dir=Math.random()<0.5?1:-1;
    const speed=isTruck?rand(1.6,2.6):rand(2.2,3.6);
    lane.vehicles.push({x:rand(-3,COLS+2), length, width:0.75, dir, speed, height:isTruck?0.7:0.5, color:randomCarColor()});
  }
}
function populateWater(lane){
  const n=randInt(2,Math.min(5,3+Math.floor(score/180)));
  for(let i=0;i<n;i++){
    const len=randInt(2,3);
    const dir=Math.random()<0.5?1:-1;
    const speed=rand(0.8,1.9);
    lane.logs.push({x:rand(-4,COLS+4), length:len, dir, speed});
  }
}
function populateGrass(lane){
  for(let col=0;col<COLS;col++) if(Math.random()<0.08) lane.flowers.push({col, color:randomFlowerColor()});
  if(Math.random()<0.35){
    const n=randInt(1,3);
    for(let i=0;i<n;i++){
      const col=randInt(0,COLS-1);
      if(lane.row===startRow && col===Math.floor(COLS/2)) continue;
      if(!lane.coins.includes(col)) lane.coins.push(col);
    }
  }
}
function populateLane(lane){
  if(lane.type==='road') populateRoad(lane);
  else if(lane.type==='water') populateWater(lane);
  else if(lane.type==='grass') populateGrass(lane);
  else if(lane.type==='rail') lane.railState={phase:'idle', timer:rand(2,4), trainX:-10, trainDir:1};
}
function addLane(r){
  const prev=rows.length?rows[rows.length-1].type:'grass';
  const type=r<=startRow?'grass':chooseType(prev);
  const lane={type,row:r,vehicles:[],logs:[],coins:[],flowers:[],railState:null,trainX:-10,trainDir:1};
  populateLane(lane);
  rows.push(lane);
}

function getLane(r){ for(let i=0;i<rows.length;i++) if(rows[i].row===r) return rows[i]; return null; }
function vehicleOverlaps(px,lane){
  const pMin=px+0.18, pMax=px+0.82;
  for(const v of lane.vehicles) if(pMax>v.x+0.05 && pMin<v.x+v.length-0.05) return true;
  return false;
}
function logUnder(px,lane){
  const pMin=px+0.18, pMax=px+0.82;
  for(const log of lane.logs) if(pMax>log.x && pMin<log.x+log.length) return log;
  return null;
}

function drawCoin(col,row){
  const cx=col+0.5, cy=row+0.5, z=0.28+Math.sin(time*7)*0.05;
  const p=iso(cx,cy,z);
  ctx.save(); ctx.translate(p.x,p.y); ctx.rotate(time*4);
  ctx.fillStyle='#ffd54f';
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(0,0,TILE_W*0.18,TILE_W*0.11,0,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
  ctx.fillStyle='#fff176';
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(-TILE_W*0.05,-TILE_W*0.03,TILE_W*0.06,TILE_W*0.04,0,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
  ctx.restore();
}
function drawVehicle(v,row){
  const y=row+0.12;
  drawBlock(v.x, y, 0, v.length, v.width, v.height, v.color);
  const headZ=v.height;
  const headColor='#fff9c4';
  if(v.dir>0) drawBlock(v.x+v.length-0.18, y+0.15, headZ, 0.14, v.width-0.3, 0.12, headColor);
  else drawBlock(v.x+0.04, y+0.15, headZ, 0.14, v.width-0.3, 0.12, headColor);
}
function drawLog(log,row){
  drawBlock(log.x, row+0.1, -0.9, log.length, 0.8, 0.28, '#8d6e63');
}
function drawTrain(lane){
  if(!lane.railState || lane.railState.phase!=='train') return;
  const len=COLS+10;
  drawBlock(lane.trainX, lane.row+0.05, 0, len, 0.9, 0.75, '#263238');
  const topZ=0.75;
  for(let i=2;i<len-1;i+=1.6) drawBlock(lane.trainX+i, lane.row+0.22, topZ, 0.6, 0.5, 0.12, '#ffeb3b');
}
function drawLane(lane){
  for(let col=0;col<COLS;col++){
    if(lane.type==='grass') drawBlock(col,lane.row,0,1,1,0.15,'#66bb6a');
    else if(lane.type==='road') drawBlock(col,lane.row,0,1,1,0.08,'#455a64');
    else if(lane.type==='water') drawBlock(col,lane.row,-2.4,1,1,1.8,'#29b6f6');
    else if(lane.type==='rail') drawBlock(col,lane.row,0,1,1,0.08,'#795548');
  }
  if(lane.type==='road'){
    ctx.globalAlpha=0.55;
    for(let col=0;col<COLS;col++) drawLine(iso(col+0.5,lane.row+0.4,0.12), iso(col+0.5,lane.row+0.6,0.12), '#fff', 2*DPR);
    ctx.globalAlpha=1;
  } else if(lane.type==='rail'){
    for(let col=0;col<COLS;col++){
      drawLine(iso(col,lane.row+0.25,0.12), iso(col+1,lane.row+0.25,0.12), '#90a4ae', 2*DPR);
      drawLine(iso(col,lane.row+0.75,0.12), iso(col+1,lane.row+0.75,0.12), '#90a4ae', 2*DPR);
      drawLine(iso(col+0.5,lane.row+0.25,0.12), iso(col+0.5,lane.row+0.75,0.12), '#5d4037', 2*DPR);
    }
    if(lane.railState && lane.railState.phase==='warning'){
      const flash=Math.sin(time*18)>0;
      drawBlock(-0.6,lane.row,0.32,COLS+1.2,0.16,0.12, flash?'#e53935':'#fff');
      drawBlock(-0.6,lane.row,0,0.3,0.3,0.55, flash?'#ff5252':'#fff');
      drawBlock(COLS+0.3,lane.row,0,0.3,0.3,0.55, flash?'#ff5252':'#fff');
    }
  } else if(lane.type==='grass'){
    lane.flowers.forEach(f=> drawBlock(f.col+0.35,lane.row+0.35,0.15,0.3,0.3,0.18,f.color));
  }
  if(lane.type==='road') lane.vehicles.forEach(v=>drawVehicle(v,lane.row));
  else if(lane.type==='water') lane.logs.forEach(log=>drawLog(log,lane.row));
  else if(lane.type==='rail') drawTrain(lane);
  lane.coins.forEach(col=>drawCoin(col,lane.row));
}
function drawShadow(cx,cy,z,scale=1){
  const p=iso(cx,cy,0);
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.22)';
  ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(p.x,p.y,TILE_W*0.28*(1-z*0.18)*scale,TILE_H*0.28*(1-z*0.18)*scale,0,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
}
function playerScale(){
  if(player.dead) return {sx:1.2, sy:0.25};
  if(!player.hopping) return {sx:1, sy:1};
  const t=player.hopT;
  if(t<0.18){ const k=t/0.18; return {sx:1+0.26*(1-k), sy:1-0.3*(1-k)}; }
  if(t>0.82){ const k=(t-0.82)/0.18; return {sx:1+0.26*k, sy:1-0.3*k}; }
  const k=Math.sin((t-0.18)/0.64*Math.PI);
  return {sx:1-0.14*k, sy:1+0.22*k};
}
function drawPlayer(){
  const cx=player.renderX+0.5, cy=player.renderY+0.5, z=player.z;
  const sc=playerScale();
  drawShadow(cx,cy,z, sc.sy<0.5?0.7:1);
  const w=0.6*sc.sx, l=0.6*sc.sx, h=0.65*sc.sy;
  const bx=cx-w/2, by=cy-l/2;
  drawBlock(bx,by,z,w,l,h,'#ffffff');
  const ez=z+h, ew=0.18, el=0.18, eh=0.34*sc.sy;
  drawBlock(cx-0.22,cy-0.1,ez,ew,el,eh,'#ffffff');
  drawBlock(cx+0.04,cy-0.1,ez,ew,el,eh,'#ffffff');
  const eyeZ=z+h+0.015;
  ctx.fillStyle='#263238';
  const left=iso(cx-0.14,cy-0.02,eyeZ), right=iso(cx+0.14,cy-0.02,eyeZ);
  const sz=TILE_W*0.11;
  ctx.fillRect(left.x-sz/2,left.y-sz/2,sz,sz);
  ctx.fillRect(right.x-sz/2,right.y-sz/2,sz,sz);
  const nose=iso(cx,cy+0.08,eyeZ);
  ctx.fillStyle='#ff8a80';
  ctx.fillRect(nose.x-sz/3,nose.y-sz/3,sz*0.7,sz*0.7);
}

function spawnSparkles(x,y){
  for(let i=0;i<12;i++){
    const a=Math.random()*Math.PI*2, sp=rand(0.5,2.2);
    particles.push({x,y,z:0.5, vx:Math.cos(a)*sp, vy:Math.sin(a)*sp, vz:rand(1,3), life:0.55, max:0.55, color:Math.random()<0.5?'#ffd54f':'#fff', size:rand(2,4.5)*DPR});
  }
}
function spawnDeathParticles(x,y){
  const cols=['#ff5252','#ffffff','#ffca28','#ff8a80','#b0bec5'];
  for(let i=0;i<38;i++){
    const a=Math.random()*Math.PI*2, sp=rand(1.5,5);
    particles.push({x,y,z:0.5, vx:Math.cos(a)*sp, vy:Math.sin(a)*sp, vz:rand(2,5.5), life:0.85, max:0.85, color:cols[randInt(0,cols.length-1)], size:rand(3,7)*DPR});
  }
}
function updateParticles(dt){
  for(let i=particles.length-1;i>=0;i--){
    const p=particles[i];
    p.x+=p.vx*dt; p.y+=p.vy*dt; p.z+=p.vz*dt;
    p.vz-=8*dt;
    p.life-=dt;
    if(p.life<=0) particles.splice(i,1);
  }
}
function drawParticles(){
  particles.forEach(p=>{
    const pos=iso(p.x,p.y,Math.max(0,p.z));
    ctx.globalAlpha=Math.max(0,p.life/p.maxLife);
    ctx.fillStyle=p.color;
    ctx.fillRect(pos.x-p.size/2,pos.y-p.size/2,p.size,p.size);
  });
  ctx.globalAlpha=1;
}

function startHop(dx,dy){
  if(state!=='playing' || player.hopping || player.dead) return;
  const ty=player.y+dy; if(ty<0) return;
  let tx;
  if(dy!==0) tx=Math.round(player.x);
  else tx=Math.round(player.x)+dx;
  if(tx<0 || tx>=COLS) return;
  player.hopping=true; player.hopT=0; player.hopDir={x:dx,y:dy};
  player.hopStartX=player.x; player.hopStartY=player.y;
  player.hopTargetX=tx; player.hopTargetY=ty;
}
function updatePlayerHop(dt){
  if(!player.hopping){ player.renderX=player.x; player.renderY=player.y; player.z=0; return; }
  player.hopT+=dt/0.18;
  if(player.hopT>=1){
    player.hopT=1;
    player.x=player.hopTargetX; player.y=player.hopTargetY;
    player.hopping=false; player.renderX=player.x; player.renderY=player.y; player.z=0;
    handleLand();
    return;
  }
  const t=player.hopT;
  player.renderX=lerp(player.hopStartX,player.hopTargetX,t);
  player.renderY=lerp(player.hopStartY,player.hopTargetY,t);
  player.z=Math.sin(t*Math.PI)*0.55;
}
function handleLand(){
  if(player.dead || state!=='playing') return;
  const lane=getLane(player.y); if(!lane) return;
  if(lane.type==='road' && vehicleOverlaps(player.x,lane)){ die(); return; }
  if(lane.type==='water' && !logUnder(player.x,lane)){ die(); return; }
  if(lane.type==='rail' && lane.railState.phase==='train'){ die(); return; }
  if(player.y>maxRow){ maxRow=player.y; score=maxRow-startRow; if(score>best){ best=score; saveBest(); } }
  const ci=lane.coins.indexOf(Math.round(player.x));
  if(ci>=0){ lane.coins.splice(ci,1); coins++; score+=5; spawnSparkles(player.x+0.5,player.y+0.5); }
  updateHUD();
}
function die(){
  if(player.dead || state==='dying' || state==='gameover') return;
  player.dead=true; state='dying'; freezeTime=0.42; shake=16;
  spawnDeathParticles(player.renderX+0.5,player.renderY+0.5);
}

function updateLanes(dt){
  const mult=1+Math.min(score,600)/180;
  rows.forEach(lane=>{
    if(lane.type==='road'){
      lane.vehicles.forEach(v=>{
        v.x+=v.speed*v.dir*dt*mult;
        if(v.dir>0 && v.x>COLS+2) v.x=-v.length-2;
        if(v.dir<0 && v.x<-v.length-2) v.x=COLS+2;
      });
    } else if(lane.type==='water'){
      lane.logs.forEach(log=>{
        log.x+=log.speed*log.dir*dt*mult;
        if(log.dir>0 && log.x>COLS+3) log.x=-log.length-3;
        if(log.dir<0 && log.x<-log.length-3) log.x=COLS+3;
      });
      if(player.y===lane.row && !player.hopping && !player.dead){
        const log=logUnder(player.x,lane);
        if(log) player.x+=log.speed*log.dir*dt*mult;
        else die();
      }
    } else if(lane.type==='rail'){
      const st=lane.railState; st.timer-=dt;
      if(st.timer<=0){
        if(st.phase==='idle'){ st.phase='warning'; st.timer=1.2; }
        else if(st.phase==='warning'){ st.phase='train'; st.timer=1.35; st.trainDir=Math.random()<0.5?1:-1; st.trainX=st.trainDir>0?-10:COLS+10; }
        else { st.phase='idle'; st.timer=rand(2,4); }
      }
      if(st.phase==='train'){
        st.trainX+=st.trainDir*14*dt;
        if(player.y===lane.row && !player.dead) die();
      }
    }
  });
}
function generateRows(){
  while(rows.length && rows[0].row<player.y-30) rows.shift();
  while(rows[rows.length-1].row<player.y+35) addLane(rows[rows.length-1].row+1);
}

function loadBest(){ try{ best=parseInt(localStorage.getItem('voxelhop_best')||'0',10)||0; }catch(e){ best=0; } }
function saveBest(){ try{ localStorage.setItem('voxelhop_best',best); }catch(e){} }
function updateHUD(){ scoreEl.textContent=score; bestEl.textContent=best; coinEl.textContent=coins; }
function showGameover(){ goScore.textContent=score; goBest.textContent=best; hud.classList.add('hidden'); gameoverScreen.classList.remove('hidden'); }

function resetGame(){
  rows=[]; particles=[]; score=0; coins=0; startRow=2; maxRow=startRow;
  const mid=Math.floor(COLS/2);
  player={x:mid,y:startRow,z:0,renderX:mid,renderY:startRow,hopping:false,hopT:0,hopDir:{x:0,y:0},hopStartX:mid,hopStartY:startRow,hopTargetX:mid,hopTargetY:startRow,dead:false};
  for(let r=0;r<=startRow+35;r++){
    addLane(r);
    if(r<=startRow){ rows[r].type='grass'; rows[r].vehicles=[]; rows[r].logs=[]; rows[r].railState=null; rows[r].coins=[]; rows[r].flowers=[]; populateGrass(rows[r]); }
  }
  cameraY=0; shake=0; freezeTime=0;
  updateHUD();
}
function initTitle(){
  rows=[];
  for(let r=0;r<10;r++){
    const lane={type:'grass',row:r,vehicles:[],logs:[],coins:[],flowers:[],railState:null,trainX:-10,trainDir:1};
    rows.push(lane); populateGrass(lane);
  }
  const mid=Math.floor(COLS/2);
  player={x:mid,y:2,z:0,renderX:mid,renderY:2,hopping:false,hopT:0,hopDir:{x:0,y:0},hopStartX:mid,hopStartY:2,hopTargetX:mid,hopTargetY:2,dead:false};
  state='title'; cameraY=0; shake=0;
}
function startGame(){
  titleScreen.classList.add('hidden');
  gameoverScreen.classList.add('hidden');
  hud.classList.remove('hidden');
  resetGame();
  state='playing';
}

function renderWorld(){
  ctx.clearRect(0,0,W,H);
  drawSky(); drawClouds();
  for(let i=rows.length-1;i>=0;i--){
    const lane=rows[i];
    drawLane(lane);
    if(state!=='title' && Math.round(player.renderY)===lane.row) drawPlayer();
  }
  drawParticles();
}

function loop(now){
  const dt=Math.min((now-lastTime)/1000,0.05); lastTime=now; time+=dt;
  resize();
  shakeX=(Math.random()-0.5)*shake; shakeY=(Math.random()-0.5)*shake;
  if(state==='title'){
    player.z=Math.sin(time*2.5)*0.18; player.renderX=player.x; player.renderY=player.y;
    updateClouds(dt);
  } else if(state==='playing' || state==='dying'){
    if(state==='playing'){
      updateLanes(dt);
      if(!player.hopping && !player.dead){
        const lane=getLane(player.y);
        if(lane){
          if(lane.type==='road' && vehicleOverlaps(player.x,lane)) die();
          else if(lane.type==='water' && !logUnder(player.x,lane)) die();
          else if(lane.type==='rail' && lane.railState.phase==='train') die();
        }
      }
      updatePlayerHop(dt);
      generateRows();
      const pBase=iso(player.renderX+0.5,player.renderY+0.5,0);
      const baseNoCam=pBase.y-cameraY;
      const targetCam=H*0.75-baseNoCam;
      cameraY=lerp(cameraY,targetCam,0.12);
    }
    updateParticles(dt); updateClouds(dt);
    if(state==='dying'){
      freezeTime-=dt; shake=Math.max(0,shake-dt*35);
      if(freezeTime<=0){ state='gameover'; showGameover(); }
    }
  } else if(state==='gameover'){
    updateParticles(dt); updateClouds(dt);
    shake=Math.max(0,shake-dt*8);
  }
  renderWorld();
  requestAnimationFrame(loop);
}

window.addEventListener('keydown',e=>{
  if(e.code==='Space'){ if(state==='title'||state==='gameover') startGame(); }
  else if(state==='playing'){
    switch(e.code){
      case 'ArrowUp': case 'KeyW': startHop(0,1); break;
      case 'ArrowDown': case 'KeyS': startHop(0,-1); break;
      case 'ArrowLeft': case 'KeyA': startHop(-1,0); break;
      case 'ArrowRight': case 'KeyD': startHop(1,0); break;
    }
  }
  if(['Space','ArrowUp','ArrowDown','ArrowLeft','ArrowRight'].includes(e.code)) e.preventDefault();
});
let touchStart=null;
window.addEventListener('touchstart',e=>{ touchStart={x:e.touches[0].clientX,y:e.touches[0].clientY}; },{passive:false});
window.addEventListener('touchmove',e=>e.preventDefault(),{passive:false});
window.addEventListener('touchend',e=>{
  if(!touchStart) return;
  const t=e.changedTouches[0];
  const dx=t.clientX-touchStart.x, dy=t.clientY-touchStart.y;
  const dist=Math.hypot(dx,dy);
  if(state==='title'||state==='gameover'){ if(dist<40 || e.target.classList.contains('btn')) startGame(); }
  else if(state==='playing' && dist>30){
    if(Math.abs(dx)>Math.abs(dy)) startHop(dx>0?1:-1,0);
    else startHop(0, dy<0?1:-1);
  }
  touchStart=null;
},{passive:false});

document.getElementById('startBtn').addEventListener('click',startGame);
document.getElementById('restartBtn').addEventListener('click',startGame);
window.addEventListener('resize',resize);

loadBest(); resize(); initClouds(); initTitle(); updateHUD();
requestAnimationFrame(loop);
</script>
</body>
</html>
```
